The Case of Wang Mo, Chief of the Tax Department, Crushed to Death by a Car, Was Settled Privately, the Public Prosecution Part Was Concluded Pending Judgment 183

Wang Mo, courtesy name Bingqing, a native of Shaoxing and chief of the Document Section of the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance, nearly sixty years old, left his residence at 9 Xinmale Lane, South Chengdu Road, at about 9 a.m. on March 21 this year and took the No. 4 tram to the Taxation Department (on the Bund, New Customs Building) to work. Just as he was getting on the tram, he was suddenly hit by a private car No. 592 driven by a chauffeur named Gao Chunsheng and owned by a Russian doctor, Mikechi. Because of his old age and serious injuries, he died despite medical treatment. The French police department transferred Gao to the Second Special District Court for prosecution on the charge of causing death by negligence in business operations. Wang Jiazhen, son of the victim, also hired a lawyer to file a private suit, seeking damages of 30,000 yuan. After the trial, Gao Chunsheng was sentenced to three years in prison and ordered to compensate the victim's family for 5,000 yuan in losses. The details have been reported in previous newspapers. It is now learned that Gao expressed dissatisfaction with the original judgment and filed an appeal with the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The High Court accepted the appeal and opened investigation hearings repeatedly. The appeal was completed. The appeal was heard on the afternoon of the day before yesterday by the collegiate panel composed of Court President Guo Dechang and judges Fan Peien and Li Shouyi. Appellant Gao Chunsheng and car owner Mikechi jointly hired three lawyers, Kong Zhaozhang, Cai Guangxiao, and Luo Jie, to defend them. Lawyer Yao Zhaodi appeared in court on behalf of the police department. The private prosecution part of the victim's family was represented by two lawyers, Tian Wenchao and You Zhi. After the trial, a settlement was reached in court regarding the private prosecution. The appellant compensated the victim's family with 2,600 yuan, approximately 1,000 yuan to be paid by the end of this month, and the remaining 1,600 yuan to be paid in two installments at the end of June and July. If payment is delayed or resisted, the amount of 5,000 yuan as ruled in the first instance will still be paid. The parties and the lawyers agreed and signed a settlement record. Regarding the public prosecution part, after mutual debate by the lawyers of both parties, the court declared the trial concluded and will set a date for sentencing.

Minutes of the First Preparatory Committee Meeting of the Chinese Merchant Marine Radio Operators' Welfare Association 187

The Chinese Merchant Marine Radio Operators' Welfare Association held its first preparatory committee meeting at 2:00 PM on the 19th at the Welfare Association of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. Attendees included preparatory committee members Shen Xibao, Ding Junyu, Xu Zifang, Dong Jingcheng, Wei Xiezhong, Zhu Shun, Liu Chengbi, Feng Diange (Qian Zaimin representing), Qiu Wukui (Li Kaifeng representing), Jiang Shangtao (Chen Songyun representing), and Xu Zhennan, Director of the Labor Guidance Section dispatched by the Maritime Workers' Special Party Branch, who attended to provide guidance. The meeting was chaired by Shen Xibao, with Zhu Shun serving as the recorder. After the formal opening ceremony, the chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting, stating that radio is a modern scientific endeavor, particularly important for maritime safety. The organization of the Welfare Association aims to achieve the following principles: In terms of academics, radio technology has made rapid progress in recent years, and service personnel should have opportunities to discuss and improve their knowledge. In terms of service, there should be adequate communication to facilitate mutual assistance in work. Radio operators serve at sea and bear significant responsibility, often sacrificing their lives in maritime disasters. However, their treatment is not always ideal, so a group organization is urgently needed to improve their livelihoods. Subsequently, Comrade Xu Zhennan, Director of the Labor Guidance Section of the Maritime Workers' Special Party Branch, delivered a speech, stating that radio operators are high-ranking sailors with heavy responsibilities. The Party Branch greatly approves of the establishment of this association and hopes that all members will strive for the overall benefit of the association. He also hopes that responsible personnel will handle matters responsibly, so that the association's affairs will prosper. He believes that all members have received higher education and will not disappoint the Party Branch's expectations. Reading Questions and Answers

Genius and Personality 199

Answering Mr. Luo Zhi, Mr. Shen Feng, and Mr. Yang Lihui

"I lack the genius to study literature." "My personality is not suitable for studying philosophy!" We often see and hear such sentences in letters from many readers and in conversations. They look with disappointed eyes at many modern writers who have "genius" and those whose "personalities" are suited for studying certain subjects. They themselves have lost confidence and lack the ambition to study literature and explore philosophical principles. They think that "genius" and "personality" are innate, just like being born to "both wealthy and noble" parents, which is completely beyond your control. They still admire these knowledge holders very much, just like beggars still salivate when they see "delicacies from land and sea." However, they can only sigh and cannot take a step forward to acquire them.

This is a very wrong concept. It hinders the progress of learning, erodes the enthusiasm of young people, and will make people give up on themselves, recognizing themselves as low-achievers who can only be content with poverty and ignorance, forever bowing their heads to those "geniuses" who control their knowledge, daring not to move even a bit.

We Must First Eliminate Mistaken Learning! 200

The natural formation of this misconception is not a simple matter; it has its social foundation and other complex factors. To enable a wider audience to understand the following explanation, we have compiled the following dialogue, based on frequently raised questions in recent letters and conversations, to aid readers in their interest in reading this communication.

- Sir! Does 'genius' exist at all, and how should it be explained?

- In my opinion, the term 'genius' should never be interpreted as innate; it is still determined by the environment of social life. You know, Edison was a great scientist, probably considered a 'genius'. He could only have been born in the 20th century, not in the Middle Ages. He could only have been born in the highly developed capitalist group of the United States, not in 'India' or 'China'?

- What do you mean by that?

- It's because Edison's inventions were not due to him having different cells in his body compared to others; his inventions were built on the conditions of scientific development in America. The conditions for nurturing his talent's development required the legacy of natural scientific knowledge from predecessors, scientific machinery equipment, and social needs. In the Middle Ages, natural scientific knowledge was insufficient, lacking the premise for his inventions. As for India and China, the colonial environment there would not allow for the emergence of such talents. Therefore, India can only produce 'Tagores,' and China currently can only produce figures like 'certain child prodigies,' whose inventions are merely 'scientific Ouija boards.' Don't laugh, if Mr. Edison of America were unfortunately born in China, he might have become a child prodigy himself, which wouldn't be surprising at all!

- Sir, don't you think that white people have higher intelligence than us? - It cannot be denied that white people generally have a higher cultural standard than us at present, but this does not mean that their race is born superior to others; it is that their social living conditions are better than ours! When it comes to the intelligence of races, there is no distinction. Currently, the capitalists among white people and the scholars they support are fabricating absurd claims that white people are superior to mixed-race people. This is nothing more than wanting to use racial superiority to rule the slaves in the colonies, so that these lackeys do not resist and willingly flatter their masters! We cannot explain Edison's inventions from the superiority of racial qualities, but only from social conditions! - Sir, I agree with the above explanation when comparing the United States and China, but why do individuals have differences in the same environment, such as in the United States or China? I always feel that 'genius' exists, and it is partly innate.

- The reasons for individual differences are very complex. There are no two identical leaves in the world. However, even the most obvious differences are caused by social conditions. Different lives create different bodies, different intellects, and different thoughts. Wealthy people eat a lot and become obese, while hungry people are inevitably thin and emaciated. Wealthy people can study from kindergarten to studying abroad, while poor people are illiterate all their lives. Wealthy people always want world peace and lasting prosperity, while poor people are afraid of the world changing - none of this is accidental. So-called 'geniuses' are all cultivated by acquired environments, not innate superior breeds. It is impossible for an illiterate person to become an Edison, and it is only a fantasy to become a Tagore because he lacks the conditions to express his abilities. For example, in the case of Mr. He, because he has not yet graduated from elementary school, he cannot appreciate literature as easily as a university student. This is because he lacks cultivation, not because his 'genius' is inferior to others. Many of today's Chinese writers have better cultivation than Mr. He, and some have been forged in hardship. Because they do not believe that 'princes and generals' have a fixed lineage, they do not believe in 'genius,' they want to struggle hard, and as a result, they have succeeded. However, there are still no writers in China who come from illiteracy, because an illiterate person must go through the stage of literacy to become a writer. If Chinese characters can be simplified immediately and illiteracy can be eliminated, then how many 'genius' writers would emerge from the people who are now considered inferior! Therefore, it is the social system that creates the current individual differences. The social environment restricts your development. It creates many different species from many homogeneous people, just as the same seed sown in the desert and fertile soil produces different results, which has little to do with the seed itself. Therefore, I say that 'genius' is not innate.

- I still have some doubts. Why do people born of the same parents and in the same small living environment have such vastly different differences?

- That's right! Such differences do exist. And differences will always exist, which means that there are no two completely identical things in the universe. But in the current society, the different intelligence of children born of the same parents is largely due to the influence of better or worse social lives in the time after each person's birth. If these reasons are ignored, the remaining differences are not bad things. Because these differences do not restrict their development but only determine their development in different directions. This is precisely enriching the universe, not artificially harming human intelligence. In short, in the future society, the words 'foolishness' and 'wisdom' will gradually be eliminated. 'Genius' will only be used as a compliment, a congratulatory speech to celebrate a successful person, not limited to the identity of a part of the people, and even less can it be interpreted as 'innate.' In the future, if there is still this term, it will be a symbol of victory that everyone can obtain. - According to your explanation, people like us who lack the conditions for development have no hope of development in this life?

- Not at all! We lack the conditions for development, and we should create conditions that are conducive to the development of our masses. For example, in your case (referring to Mr. He), since you have graduated from elementary school and want to study literature, the road to development is certainly very difficult, but it does not mean that you cannot open a path. What is problematic here is not the objective difficulties, but the errors in your concepts. If you believe that 'princes and generals' must come from 'the houses of princes and generals,' that you yourself are a mediocre seed, lacking some kind of 'genius,' then you naturally have no determination to conquer the environment, and you will inevitably erode the vitality of your life in this concept. If you have a transformation in your concepts, you may use the conditions permitted in your current living range to advance step by step. If you want to become a writer, you can actually experience life and cultivate your writing skills at the same time, and you can naturally hope to open up a path in literature. Even for an illiterate person, as long as he is not content with 'fate,' he will naturally rise up, first improving his minimum living standard, and when his life improves, he will demand to expand his knowledge, demand to be literate and read, and he will also demand that others can do any part of the social work that he can also engage in. Therefore, we feel that you are not hopeless in this life, but it depends on whether you work hard!

- I understand everything now. The level of intelligence is entirely determined by social reasons and the degree to which you strive to conquer the environment. The so-called 'genius' is not something that ordinary people cannot achieve, but it is just that others either do not have the opportunity or are unwilling to fight. Sir, do you think that's right?

- That's right! Do you have any other questions?

- No. I originally had another question, which is the difference in personality. Now that I have heard your explanation of the term 'genius,' this question has also been solved in connection. 'Personality' is naturally also cultivated by the environment, isn't it?

- Yes!

- Then, personality should also be changeable. I often hear many friends say that one's personality is close to literature and that most of them do not understand mathematics. Now I feel that since personality can be changed by the environment, can't a person who studies literature also become someone who likes to study mathematics?

- Of course! Many young people now have a misunderstanding about personality. They do not understand what personality is. They think that whatever is easy to study is close to their personality, otherwise it is not close. Therefore, your friends think that literature and social sciences are easy to study and require less effort. Mathematics requires performing problems and following step-by-step procedures, so it is more difficult. In fact, many people regard learning as too cheap, and when they encounter difficulties, they think it is not close to their personality, so they abandon what they are studying halfway. In fact, literature and social sciences are no easier than mathematics and require hard work. Personality is certainly cultivated by the environment, but it cannot be determined that one's personality is not close based on a shallow attempt at knowledge. It is right to value the conditions suitable for one's own research, and there is no need to force oneself to pursue it if there are no conditions for learning chemistry, but it is wrong to determine that it is not suitable for one's own personality because of difficulties. Because personality is determined by the environment, it can naturally be transformed. For example, the Chinese masses currently need to understand the national crisis and international politics, but they cannot ignore the knowledge that citizens should have because of some personality that is not close to it. How should we transform it, make it interested in ourselves, and change the reasons that caused this neglect of politics and avoidance of practice? As for those whose living conditions are suitable for advancing in a certain field of knowledge, in addition to not ignoring common knowledge, other specialties can be freely developed by him, and there is no need to force each other, nor is there any reason to force him to switch to a certain special field of knowledge.

Chun Qiu

The Fragrant Cloud Records of Imperial Incense 201

- Original work by Princess Der Ling of Qing, translated by Qin Shouou

The interior of the imperial carriage was entirely draped with apricot-yellow tribute silk. The colors of these silks were particularly vibrant and were frequently changed. When the Empress Dowager was about to use it, Li Lianying would personally go over and carefully examine it. If there were any stains or missing items, he would immediately have them repaired or replaced. When the Empress Dowager entered the imperial carriage, a cloth curtain would be temporarily added around it, so that no one could peek at her. Even the eunuchs assigned to carry this imperial carriage could not see her. Only after she was seated securely in the imperial carriage was the cloth curtain removed; at the same time, the porters carefully took on this heavy burden. If, unfortunately, one of the porters took a wrong step, causing the Empress Dowager in the imperial carriage to fall, or even if she didn't fall but was frightened, it would be a major incident! At most, within half a day, the heads of these sixteen porters would all be hanging down! However, as far as I know, such a thing has never actually happened: because the sixteen porters who carried this imperial carriage for the Empress Dowager could be said to be the best of the best selected from tens of thousands of porters in China. In any case, they would never take a wrong step. They themselves were often very proud and thought that being able to serve the Empress Dowager was truly the most glorious thing. Their clothing was also very beautiful: they wore ordinary skullcaps, but without any decorations such as tops or feathers! They wore a light red vest on their upper body; below, they wore lake-green trousers; on their feet were dark black boots, but not long ones.

Whether starting or walking, they were very careful; of course, they knew that being beheaded was not an interesting thing! (38)

Wrath Silences Han 202

There is an ancient saying: "Wrath is a fierce tiger, desire is a deep abyss." Getting angry is indeed very harmful to the body. According to research by psychologists, when people are angry, all functions stop. If you lose your temper while eating, it will make you unable to eat. Therefore, Napoleon also said: People who cannot form a habit of self-control cannot have healthy bodies. To curb anger, we can only work hard on the word "patience." If patience is achieved, anger will naturally be curbed. The Western philosopher Cicero said: "We must conquer anger as we conquer a strong enemy." Gifford Johnson also said: "When angry, count from one to ten before speaking. When very angry, count from one to one hundred." These statements are nothing more than calling on rude people to do more patience. A passage recorded in ancient books is very worth introducing: When Fu Bi was young, someone scolded him, and he pretended not to hear. Someone said: "He is scolding you." Bi said: "I am afraid he is scolding someone else." He also said: "He is calling your name." Bi said: "I am afraid it is someone with the same name." The man was very ashamed.

We young people with vigor and vitality are most prone to getting angry. We might as well learn from Fu Bi, but we must remember: "The anger of blood and qi cannot be had, but the anger of righteousness and reason cannot be without."

The Substitute Rickshaw Puller 203

- Fu Yizhi

My friend Mr. W called me and asked me to go to his place - Rue Mercier. Because time was very tight, I hailed a rickshaw on Rue du Consulat and got on. The elastic rubber wheels rolled silently on the smooth asphalt road - Avenue Dubail, especially without shaking. My eyes slowly surveyed the residences, fences, tiger stoves, incense paper shops, and indistinct pedestrians along the way, feeling infinitely leisurely and comfortable, more so than those sitting in cars!

"Avenue Dubail!"

"Ah! Avenue Dubail!"

On the movable iron tongs of the rickshaw's canopy hung a Jiangbei man who looked like a rickshaw puller, which I could tell from his accent. He pulled the iron tongs and followed the rickshaw closely. The rickshaw puller turned his head and said the name of the road to him, and he squeezed out a sentence very concernedly

"Rue de la Porte de France!"

When we arrived at Rue de la Porte de France, the rickshaw puller called out the street sign as usual: but there was no response, was he panting too hard to squeeze out a word, or did he understand and take it for granted? I didn't ask about Pont de France, Rue de Zikawei, Rue du Marché, Rue Bayle. The rickshaw puller called out as usual, but with a slightly hoarse voice, not as loud as at the beginning; therefore, sometimes he "understood tacitly," and sometimes he could only make a couple of echoes from the bottom of his throat. After passing Lokawei, even the rickshaw puller didn't announce it publicly. Undoubtedly, that was because he himself was also "baffled," because he was asking me where to run,

No matter how small a "trade" is, if we are not "hereditary" or "noble," and we want to make it a career, we should put in some practical effort and spend a sum of expected losses. This substitute rickshaw puller wasted precious time and exhausted his strength, just for the sake of future gains. There is nothing in sight. I thought,

The Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 204

- Zhang Henshui

Chapter 29 - Returning to the Injured Foot, Sadness, Solitary Survival, Listening to Hua, Greed, Blood Oath, Common Loyalty

When Yang Guizhi received Gan Binzhi's letter, she knew that something was not right, but refusing to accept it and holding each other at the gate would only make things worse if a second person saw it. So, regardless of everything, she quickly took the letter from Lianjiang. From Binzhi's point of view, he believed that where there is a will, there is a way, and he didn't feel anything strange, but Guizhi was determined to leave Binzhi. Binzhi giving her such a letter, she naturally regarded it as a kind of demon. It was not only shy, but also considered extremely immoral. Therefore, she didn't bother to delay at the gate and turned around and went back to her house. Fortunately, Zhao Weng was not at home, so she closed the door and read Binzhi's letter from beginning to end. After reading it, she couldn't help but sneer and say to herself: Isn't this a dream? She took the letter in her hand and pondered it quietly, thinking that this matter should not be concealed from her mother. If she told her directly, and if there was any turmoil, the mother and son could discuss it together. Having an older person to direct them would always provide more knowledge. So, without hesitation, she took the letter and rushed to Jiang's room, raised the letter, and said with a calm face: Mom! Look, isn't this a joke? Gan Er Ye wrote a letter to me in good faith, rambling and saying a lot. Jiang's face immediately turned red, and she gasped and said; What are you looking at? What are you shouting about? Saying that, she stood up and rushed to close the door first. Only then did she whisper: This is nonsense. He wrote a letter to you, what did he say in the letter? Read it to me. Guizhi blushed and didn't read the letter first, but said with a taut face; This is really a joke. (388)

Production Survey Anecdotes 205

- Youzhi

In order to understand the actual situation of the rural economy and to find a possible way out, our school held a rural production survey. Although we solemnly conveyed the motives and purposes of our survey to the farmers in advance, the following incident still occurred on the first day.

"Sir! Thank you! Don't write us down in the book!" An old farmer who was nearly fifty years old begged us tremblingly.

"Uncle! It doesn't matter, it doesn't cost you any money. This is held in our school, and we can guarantee it!" I said sincerely to him.

"Alas! Sir! Some time ago, someone from the town went to the countryside, nailed a piece of foreign lead skin on my door, and asked us for a string of money! Also, my said that if your names are written down, the superiors will come to arrest you to fight the Communists!" he said.

"Isn't it? You are going to ask clearly how many acres of land we have, how many , that's not okay! It is said that even one chicken costs three hundred coins!" Another person came out and said.

After repeated explanations, they let us fill it in. But they made the final request; don't go up to the ! Sir!

Artistic Traces

Travels in Yanzhou 207

- Chen Shicheng

Yanzhou is located in the upper reaches of the Zhijiang River, thirty miles from Xukou. It goes east to Wuling, west to Shexian County, and south to Lanxi. It has important transportation routes. Since the completion of the Hangzhou-Jiang Railway, its situation has changed. I and Hu Ziboxiang and others traveled to the Seven-Li Rapids. When the boat reached Yancheng, it was already eight bells down. I heard that the motorboat stopped at Yandongguan, about three miles from the city. You have to walk there. Now it has been raining for a long time and the water has risen, so you can reach Yancheng directly. Abandoning the boat to go ashore, we went to Wang Wanchun for dinner together.

Yancheng has a dangerous terrain and fertile land. It is a rich country. In recent years, the low price of grain has harmed farmers, and the income is only enough to pay taxes, resulting in the decline of all industries, the poverty of the people, and the exhaustion of wealth. Our country, China, is based on agriculture, and Jiangzhe is known for its prosperity, but rural bankruptcy is so, and the many bandits are well-founded. We set off at half past seven on the morning of the 31st. Leaving the east gate and turning right, we arrived at Qilang Temple at a quarter past eight. The temple is built facing the river, with a majestic momentum. The door has a plaque that says "Ancient Jianchang Hall." The hall enshrines the spirit of Anle King Qilang. To the right of the temple is the Jianjiang Pavilion, a pavilion tower, which can be climbed to view the scenery. Looking south at the Qiantang River, the waves

It is as flat as a mirror, with mountains facing each other, and distant trees containing smoke. Those who are open-minded and happy will stay for a long time.

Leaving the temple at five past eight, we crossed the river and headed towards Nangaofeng. There is a Xun Pagoda on the top of the peak, named because the land is located in the Xun position of Yancheng. At five past ten, we arrived at Tianning Temple. The temple is located next to the pagoda and is very simple. We went to climb the pagoda together. The pagoda is built of bricks, and only five floors can be climbed, with sixteen to twenty steps per floor. Looking north at Yancheng, it is like living at the bottom of a cauldron. According to the words of various physiognomists, it is also a blessed place. Downstairs, we went to the temple to ask for tea to quench our thirst. The monks in the temple offered pickled vegetables and salted radishes, which tasted very delicious. In a moment, all the utensils were eaten up. Asked about its method, it was only to put the radish at the bottom of the vat when pickling vegetables in winter. The abbot's name is Gongyuan, who is amiable and kind, but his face is pale. At eleven o'clock, we hired a small boat to cross the boat. The boat is narrow and long like a shuttle, without a cabin. There were eight people in the same company, and it was almost impossible to accommodate them. At forty past eleven, we arrived at Yandongguan, landed and had a meal at Taste My Home. After that, the group climbed Beigaofeng.

The peak is outside Yandongguan, and the land is located in the Mao position of Yancheng, so the tower on the top of the peak is named after Mao. It stands opposite Nangaofeng across the river. At ten past two, we left Yandongguan, and the peak was already towering in front of us. The mountain is steep and narrow, and the road is narrow like a sheep intestine, winding and circling in a zigzag shape. We mustered up our courage to climb, but before reaching the waist of the book, we were already panting and unable to stop. At thirty-five past two, we arrived at Tonggu Temple. The temple faces the river with its back to the mountain, and the momentum is very magnificent. There is a couplet on the palace by Liu Zongbiao of Xiling: "Pulling up a lone peak, opening the auspiciousness of the third yuan of the imperial examination." "A pillar that shocks the sky, locking the waves of ten thousand hectares of the river." The couplet seems to refer to something, but unfortunately the monks in the temple do not understand the meaning of the text, so they asked and could not answer. The abbot's name is Pucang, a lay Buddhist who guards the temple, using a stick as a guide, and went to visit Maota. The tower is also built of bricks, towering on the top of the peak, about ten feet higher than the temple, and all seven floors can be climbed. At ten past two, we arrived at the top of the tower, overlooking the Qiantang River, winding like a belt, and the creek meandering from the south, meeting in front of the peak. Looking north at Wulong, it is majestic and beautiful, surrounded by mountains, like a tiger crouching and a dragon盘, the smoky trees are blurred, presenting a group of dark colors, and the sailing walls are looming, sometimes going and sometimes coming, a natural picture is exhausted.

Turning down, we followed the old road. The road is narrow and winding, and the soil is mostly sandy, making it slippery and not leaving enough feet. At thirty-five past three, we arrived at the Immortal Well. The well is located in the east of the temple, with two mouths, arranged side by side like human eyes. The water is slightly white. Pucang said that the source of the North Well is Creek, and the source of the South Well is Zhengzhou. Although they are located side by side in the mountains, their clarity is different. Looking at it, it is true. Mountain residents have difficulty in fetching water, so they get this good convenience. The strangeness of creation is all the more convincing.

At ten past four, we returned to Yancheng, and entered Xingren Gate at a quarter past five. Donghu is already in sight. There are six hospitals and the Yanziling Ancestral Temple. Most of the houses are built in Western style. To the right is West Lake, which is smaller than East Lake. After browsing for a moment, we left and returned.

Special Issue of the 10th Far Eastern Games

Unhappy Closing of the Far Eastern Games: Our Delegation Withdraws from the Executive Committee, Firmly Expressing Opposition to the Illegal Amendment of the Charter. Disappointing Basketball Championship Loss to the Philippines Last Night. Our Country Wins Football Championship 4-3 Against Japan. 208

The 10th Far Eastern Games concluded yesterday. During the Executive Committee meeting, our country's representatives, unwilling to accept illegal pressure, collectively withdrew. The outcome regarding the amendment of the charter resulted in a stalemate. While the Philippines agreed to our country maintaining Article 3 of the charter, which stipulates that "the admission of new member states requires the unanimous approval of existing member states," they also proposed amending Article 10 of the charter, which would allow non-member states to participate in exhibition matches. Our country firmly opposed this, leading to a heated debate. Our representatives resolutely withdrew midway through the meeting. Although the Japanese and Philippine representatives continued the meeting, no concrete results were achieved. Japan even declared the dissolution of the congress last night. The Executive Committee also passed many motions. Women's tennis, volleyball, swimming, diving, shooting, boxing, and wrestling will all be upgraded to official championship events starting from the next Games. In the all-around competition, the 3000-meter steeplechase will be added, and a 5000-meter long-distance run will be added to the track and field events. All competition events of yesterday's congress, except for tennis, where only three groups were held (the Philippines led 2-1), which still need to be completed today, have been resolved. In the football final, our country defeated Japan 4-3, retaining this sole championship. In the China-Philippines basketball final, although our country fought hard in the first half (a 20-20 tie), the Philippine team ultimately defeated us 44-33. The championship continued to be won by the Philippines. The Philippines-Japan baseball final ended in a 2-2 tie and was terminated due to darkness, resulting in the championship being awarded to the Philippines. In the China-Philippines women's tennis exhibition, each side won once. Our national team is scheduled to return on the 23rd and is expected to arrive in Shanghai on the morning of the 28th. The long-anticipated 10th Far Eastern Games have thus come to a close.

Opposing the Illegal Amendment of the Charter

Our Representatives Resolutely Leave the Venue. The Philippines Proposes Amending Article 10, Allowing Non-Member Countries to Participate in Exhibitions. The Compromise Clearly Shows Collusion. Japan Even Declares the Dissolution of the Far Eastern Games. 209

(Central News Agency, Manila, 20th) The Far Eastern Athletic Association Committee continued its meeting at the Columbia Club at 10:00 AM on the 20th. Those in attendance included Honorary President Ryozo Hiranuma, Chinese representatives Shen Siliang, Hao Gengsheng, and Ma Yuehan, Japanese representatives Matsuzawa, Abe, and Shibuya, Philippine representatives Bumbucanao, Schnees, and Arras, Chairman Vargas, Secretary Ylaran. The Dutch East Indies were not present. Members of various subcommittees also participated. The reports of the various subcommittees were discussed and passed after amendments. The discussion was completed at 1:15 PM.

The Philippines Argues to Maintain Article 3 210

Then, the issue of amending the charter was discussed, and the atmosphere at the meeting immediately became tense. First, Philippine representative Arras reported on the proceedings of the two special committee meetings on the 19th, stating that all parties had engaged in friendly and open discussions but could not reach a result. It was decided that each representative would submit a separate report to the congress. The Philippine side's opinion was that Article 3 of the charter should be maintained, requiring unanimous approval from all members for the admission of new members. However, Article 10 could be amended to allow the host country to invite non-member countries to participate in competitions. The Dutch East Indies and Annam were regarded as non-member countries. Arras's report lasted fifteen minutes before it was completed.

Hao Says the Charter Does Not Need Amendment 211

Next, Chinese representative Hao Gengsheng reported, stating that the Japanese side proposed amending Article 3 of the charter to allow more new members to join. The Far Eastern Games have been established for over twenty years, and the spirit has always been good. After the passage of Article 3, two new members, the Dutch East Indies and Annam, have already joined without difficulty. Therefore, there is no problem with Article 3, and the charter does not need amendment. The Japanese proposal is particularly puzzling, he said. This lasted twelve minutes before completion.

Japanese Representatives Are At A Loss For Words 212

Japanese representative Abe then spoke, reiterating that the addition of new members would make the congress even more vibrant. Furthermore, this matter is very small, so why does China insist on it? His words were extremely clumsy and devoid of reason, so he finished in only seven minutes.

Hao Gengsheng Rebukes Him Sharply 213

Hao Gengsheng rose again to refute the Japanese representative's remarks, stating that the admission of new members is not hindered by the charter. Since the Japanese side claims that amending the charter is a trivial matter, then why propose it and why insist on it?

We Do Not Agree to Participation in Competitions 214

Shen Siliang stated that he agreed with the Philippine representative Arras's proposal to maintain Article 3. However, amending Article 10 to allow non-member countries to participate in competitions seems to violate the principle of Article 3 of the charter, and China cannot agree to it.

The Chairman Proposes a Temporary Recess 215

Chairman Vargas proposed a temporary recess of several minutes for Hao Gengsheng, Arras, and Abe to hold another meeting. The three representatives consulted for about ten minutes before reconvening.

Our Side Opposes Holding a Vote 216

Vargas advocated holding a vote on the Philippine proposal. Shen Siliang solemnly declared his opposition, stating that if Article 10 is amended, it would completely contradict the purpose of Article 3. Furthermore, the Japanese side's purpose in proposing to amend Article 3 is to increase membership. If the Philippine proposal is adopted, wouldn't the Dutch East Indies and Annam, which have already been recognized as members, be turned into non-members? This is completely inconsistent with both the principles of justice and the spirit of amending the charter.

A Minority Should Not Oppress the Majority 217

Furthermore, even if other articles are amended, they must be passed by a two-thirds majority of all members. Currently, only three member states are present. China has already opposed the amendment. If the Philippines and Japan agree to the amendment, only two members agree, which means that a minority is oppressing the majority, completely violating the spirit of the charter. China absolutely cannot bear this responsibility, Shen concluded.

Our Proposal to Submit to the World Congress 218

Abe spoke in favor of Arras's proposal. Vargas again intended to hold a vote. Shen Siliang stood up again to object, speaking eloquently with a strong attitude and sufficient reasoning. He also proposed that the issue of amending the charter be submitted to the World Sports Congress for resolution, or that a separate committee to amend the charter be convened for discussion at the next Games.

Our Country's Representatives Withdraw En Masse 219

The Japanese side expressed opposition. Our country's representatives were greatly angered and stated that if the meeting insisted on amending the charter passed by all members with the agreement of a minority, China could not bear this responsibility and could only withdraw from today's meeting to demonstrate its support for the spirit of the charter. Shen also stated that China would still invite all countries to participate in the next Games in Shanghai. After speaking, all of our representatives withdrew at 3:30 PM.

Japanese and Philippine Parties Hold Private Meetings 220

Japan and the Philippines continued to meet for one hour and resolved: (1) Article 10 of the Far Eastern Athletic Association charter, as proposed by Arras, should be amended. The championship competitions of the Far Eastern Games are limited to amateur athletes from member associations and countries permitted to participate. (2) If China is unable to host the next Games, they will be held in Tokyo. (3) A meeting will be convened next year to discuss the charter and matters related to the next Games.

Extremely Absurd: The Philippines' Compromise Proposal. Maintain Article 3, Amend Article 10. Non-Member Countries May Participate in Exhibitions. 221

(Dentsu News Agency, Manila, 20th) The regular congress, which was on the verge of collapse, convened at the Columbia Club at 10:30 AM today. Today was the second day of the congress. The Dutch East Indies had already returned home yesterday and were therefore absent today. First, the report of the Constitutional Committee from last night was presented. This was to make the Japanese proposal to amend the constitution an addendum to the constitution. Therefore, Japanese committee member Abe immediately stated that the amendment to the constitution was not an addendum and requested a correction, which was acknowledged by the entire congress. Following the review of the committee report, Dr. Vargas first declared, "Before discussing the constitutional issue, I hope to discuss the technical issues." The proposal was unanimously supported. The technical committee reported:

1. The organization of the competition committee shall be irrespective of nationality.

2. Track and field athletics will continue with the three championship systems of track, field, and all-around. The 5000-meter race will be included in the track events.

3. The 3000-meter steeplechase will be included in the all-around competition and will be held on the second day of the competition. The decision was passed without objection. Reports from the swimming, basketball, volleyball, and football committees were also presented. At 12:40 PM, the constitutional issue was finally addressed. First, Philippine committee member Arras of the Constitutional Committee reported on the proceedings of the Constitutional Committee last night, stating that due to differences of opinion, the committee's report could not be produced. The amendment proposed by Japan was to abolish the clause in Article 3 that requires unanimous approval for the admission of new members and to add clauses stating that it should be based on a two-thirds majority of those attending the congress or the unanimous agreement of the executive committee. After a break, the meeting reconvened. The Philippines proposed another amendment, that Article 3 of the constitution, which stipulates that all must vote unanimously to admit new member countries, need not be amended. However, Article 10 should be amended to allow sovereign countries outside the member countries to be invited to the congress on behalf of a generation of coordination between China and Japan regarding the frontal conflict over Article 3. Japan supported the new Philippine proposal, but the Chinese side strongly opposed and refuted the Philippine proposal, stating that according to the Far Eastern Athletic Association League rules, amending the constitution requires a two-thirds vote of all representatives at the regular congress. Now that the Dutch East Indies have returned home and Annam is not present, it does not reach two-thirds, and they strongly rejected it. Regarding the Japanese and Philippine proposals, both Japan and the Philippines reiterated that the so-called two-thirds refers to two-thirds of those attending the congress, which is obviously sufficient. Thereupon, the Chinese side, because it needed to argue again, said that China absolutely opposes it. Although the competition in progress will continue to participate, but the matter has come to this, there is no need to stay in the congress, and the Chinese side left together. The meeting was then held only by Japan and the Philippines. The Japanese side then requested a decision on the amendment to Article 3, but was rejected by the Philippines. As a result, the amendment to Article 10 in the Philippine proposal was passed without objection. Furthermore, at the eleventh congress in 1938, the Chinese side had proposed to hold the meeting in Shanghai. However, given the current situation, it is possible that China may withdraw from the Far Eastern Congress, so Japan requested that the 1938 congress be held in Japan. The Philippines replied that since the Chinese side had made a request first, it was difficult to change it. If the central government does not implement the request to hold the meeting in Shanghai, then the meeting can be held in Japan. Japan had no choice but to agree. Furthermore, since other amendments still need to be reviewed, it was decided to convene a temporary congress at the end of this year or in the spring of next year and adjourned.

Illegally Passed: Our Country Resolutely Opposes. The Agreement of Two-Thirds of All Members Should Include Annam and the Dutch East Indies. 222

(Dentsu News Agency, Manila, 20th) After the report of Philippine Constitutional Committee member Arras at today's Far Eastern Athletic Association regular congress, Chinese representative Hao Gengsheng said, "According to the current constitution, the Dutch East Indies and Annam are newly joined countries, and the current constitution is not inconsistent. However, Japan has proposed amendments, and I don't know what the true constitution is." Japanese representative Abe replied, "Japan proposed the amendment for the prosperity of the congress, but the Chinese committee members opposed this clause, which is difficult to understand." Representative Hao Gengsheng elaborated in detail that the constitution has no defects. At that time, the meeting was adjourned for lunch and reconvened in the afternoon. The Philippines proposed a motion: "Do not amend Article 3 of the constitution, amend Article 10 (China, Japan, and the Philippines are full member countries, and all other countries are participating countries)." The Chinese side stated that Article 14 of the constitution states that amendments to the constitution require the consent of more than two-thirds of the representatives of the regular congress. Therefore, it should be interpreted as two-thirds of the entire group of China, Japan, the Philippines, Annam, and the Dutch East Indies. At that time, the committee members from Japan and the Philippines said, "The interpretation of two-thirds of the countries attending the congress is correct. Regardless of the rules of procedure, the principle of adopting a majority of those present is adopted to establish a principle. If the number of absentees is added, such an interpretation has never been heard before." The Chinese representative then said that he was not responsible for the decision against the constitution. Thereupon, the Chinese committee members left the chamber together, at 2:45 PM. Afterwards, only the committee members from Japan and the Philippines remained. Therefore, if the constitution is not amended, the counterfeit country will not have formal member country qualifications. Therefore, the Japanese side waited until this congress was completed before dissolving the current Far Eastern Congress and organizing a new competition association. It requested the understanding of the Philippines. The Philippine side unofficially agreed to this proposal. The various clauses decided by Japan and the Philippines today are as follows:

(1) Article 3 of the constitution is not amended. Newly participating countries are not called full member countries, but are invited to attend and compete for the championship.

(1) A special congress to amend the constitution is scheduled to be held at the end of this year or in the spring of next year.

Japanese Representative Declares Dissolution of the Congress 223

(Japan United Press, Manila, 20th) The Japanese delegation, because its proposal to amend Article 3 of the charter was unsuccessful, declared the dissolution of the congress tonight.

A Penalty Kick Determines Fate: Our Country Wins the Football Championship

4-3: We Led 3-1 When Li Tiansheng Was Sent Off. Japan Tied 3-3, Fortunately Hui Tang Scored a Penalty. Tan Jiangbai Was the Hero of Our Team. 224

(Our Newspaper, Manila, 20th Dispatch) Our country won the football championship, defeating Japan 4-3 yesterday afternoon, achieving a record of three wins in three matches. In the first half, Tan Jiangbai scored consecutive goals, giving our country a 2-0 lead. After leading 3-1 in the second half, our country's key defender, Li Tiansheng, was sent off, and the situation immediately became tense. Japan took the opportunity to invade twice, tying the score at 3-3. Finally, our country's star player, Li Huitang, scored a penalty kick, defeating Japan 4-3. The match unfolded as follows:

Tan Jiangbai Scores with a Header 225

Japan kicked off, and our army immediately took the offensive, launching a major attack. Japan was forced to retreat and defend tenaciously. Our army besieged relentlessly. After five minutes, Liang Rongzhao sent a high ball from behind. Tan Jiangbai accurately judged the ball's trajectory, calmly jumped up, and scored the first goal.

Hui Tang Misses a Penalty 226

After scoring the first goal, the four stands erupted in cheers. Our country continued to make progress, not yielding in the slightest. While besieging in front of the goal, the Japanese team's left defender touched the ball with his hand, resulting in a penalty. Li Huitang took the kick, but unfortunately, he used too little force, and the ball rolled along the ground. The Japanese goalkeeper caught it, which was a great pity.

The Flying General Descends from the Sky 227

Continuing to persevere and apply pressure, Li Huitang intercepted the ball and sent it flying to the right. The ball went very high. Tan Jiangbai aimed at the ball and flew towards it. In the blink of an eye, Tan Jiangbai scored again. It was exactly fifteen minutes after the start of the match. Our army then took a 2-0 lead. The first half also ended.

The Japanese Army Fights Like Cornered Beasts 228

After the half-time break, the Japanese army showed some improvement and repeatedly fought like cornered beasts. After fifteen minutes, they harassed in front of the goal continuously. Huang Jiliang received the ball, but in the midst of the chaos, he threw it not far enough. The Japanese army's right inside forward lightly lifted it and kicked it in, making it 2-1.

Li Tiansheng Is Actually Sent Off 229

Five minutes later, our army still had the advantage, attacking the enemy. Li Huitang kicked a high ball, which landed in the net. Although the Japanese goalkeeper jumped up to save the ball, his hand brushed against it, but it still entered the goal. Unexpectedly, at this time, our army's main defender, Li Tiansheng, was penalized by the referee for violating the rules and was sent off. After this blow, our army's defense line was greatly shaken.

The Score Is Tied at 3-3 230

The Japanese army seized this opportunity, deploying all its forces. Our country was caught off guard and was actually scored against three times in five minutes. However, one of the goals was scored by hand, which the referee disallowed. After this change, a 3-3 tie was suddenly created between China and Japan.

A Penalty Kick Establishes Dominance 231

The situation suddenly became tense, and both sides fought to the death. Our army used all its might, pressing fiercely towards the enemy's阵. During another siege, the Japanese army's right defender was again seen touching the ball with his hand. Therefore, our team had another chance to score a penalty. Li Huitang, learning from the past, used an extremely powerful shot. The goalkeeper was helpless. As a result, our country won 4-3.

Tan Jiangbai Is the Hero 232

Tan Jiangbai was the hero of our team, scoring consecutive goals in the first half.

His performance was the most satisfactory. Li Huitang did not show any special characteristics. The Japanese team's skills were mediocre and far inferior to ours. However, their stamina and fighting spirit were unmatched by other countries. Awards Given Yesterday 234

(Dentsu News Agency, Manila, 20th) The tenth Far Eastern Games have now come to a successful conclusion. Therefore, the closing ceremony will be held tonight. This afternoon, during the break of the football match, Vice President Vargas presented awards to the selected athletes from the track and field competitions.

The Executive Committee Passed This Morning: Three More Championships to Be Added in the Next Games

Diving and Women's Swimming and Volleyball. Steeplechase Added to All-Around. Long Distance Race Added to Track and Field. 235

(Japan United Press, Manila, 30th) The Executive Committee held its second day of meetings at 10:00 AM this morning. All those in attendance were the same as yesterday's meeting, except for the Dutch East Indies representatives who returned home yesterday. First, the results of the review of the proposals submitted yesterday by the various committees were reported. After the representatives of China and the Philippines proposed some amendments, they were passed. Then, the various competition issues were reviewed. The Japanese proposal to form a competition committee by foreign committee members other than the host country was rejected. Other decisions are as follows:

Swimming Matters 236

(1) The 50-meter race will be cancelled. (2) A women's championship will be established. (3) The order of the competition program will be changed as follows: Day 1: 100-meter freestyle, 200-meter breaststroke; Day 2: 400-meter freestyle, 100-meter backstroke, 1500-meter freestyle. If preliminary rounds are necessary, the finals will be held the next day. (4) The springboard competition will be incorporated into the official championship competition. (5) Swimming events will be held on the same day for both male and female athletes. (6) A quick command will be used for the starting order.

Track and Field All-Around 237

(1) A 3000-meter steeplechase event will be added to the all-around competition and will be held on the second day of the all-around competition. (2) A 5000-meter race will be added to the track and field competition. (3) The current regulation for the high jump, which is the eighth event, will be changed to the sixth event. (4) The long jump, which is the sixth event, will be changed to the eighth event. The order of the pole vault event will be changed. (5) The 400-meter relay will be held first on the first day. (6) In the track and field program on the second day, the pole vault will be the second event, and the shot put will be the fourth event. (7) The 3000-meter steeplechase will be held first on the fourth day.

Other Matters 238

(1) The number of team members in the basketball regulations will be changed to twelve. (2) Each country will have four athletes participating in one event, with one designated as a reserve. (3) Women's volleyball will be changed to an official championship event. The number of team members will be fifteen. (4) The holding of an overtime in football will be limited to one time. (5) The competition time can be changed. (6) The issue of increasing referees will be in accordance with international congress regulations. (7) The prizes for each sport will not be newly manufactured in the future, and efforts will be made to gradually reduce their number. The Philippines Retains Basketball Supremacy. In Last Night's Final, Our Country Lost to the Philippines 33-44. Our Country Led All the Way in the First Half but Ended in a 20-20 Tie. 239

(Our Newspaper, Manila, 20th Dispatch) Our country's basketball team competed in the final against the Philippines at the Santo Tomas basketball court tonight and unfortunately lost 33-44 to the Philippines. The first half ended in a 20-20 tie. Our country led all the way in the first half, 8-8, then 15-13, our country was ahead by two points. At 20-19, the Philippine team scored another point with a free throw, making it 20-20. Tang Baokun did not play in the second half because he had committed three fouls in the first half. The Philippines only began to use its official lineup in the second half, so the score difference gradually widened, resulting in a final score of 44-33. Chen Shengkui performed well for our team, with quick and impressive movements.

(Dentsu News Agency, Manila, 20th) The second China-Philippines basketball match was held at the Santo Tomas College basketball court at 8:00 PM this afternoon. Both armies fought desperately. The Chinese army's momentum was stronger in the first half, resulting in a 20-20 tie. Unfortunately, they failed to maintain their momentum in the second half and were overwhelmed by the Philippine army. As a result, the Philippine army won 44-33.

The Philippines Wins the Baseball Championship. The Philippines-Japan Final Ends in a 2-2 Tie Due to Darkness. 240

(Dentsu News Agency, Manila, 20th) The second Philippines-Japan baseball match began at 2:00 PM this afternoon, with the Japanese army starting on offense. The Japanese army's pitcher was Kikutani, and the catcher was Tezuka. The Philippine army's pitcher was Almonte, and the catcher was Casimiro. The Japanese army scored one point in the first inning. The Philippine army also scored two points. Afterwards, neither army scored any points. In the ninth inning, the Japanese army scored another point, tying the score. Therefore, a rematch was necessary. In the tenth inning, neither army scored any points, but it was already dark. The judge then declared the game stopped. As a result, the championship was awarded to the Philippine army, which had three wins and no losses.

Unexpected Results in Tennis Finals, Philippines Take Advantage 253

One Singles, One Doubles

Japan Suffers Complete Defeat

- Competition Continues Today -

The Philippines-Japan tennis finals were repeatedly postponed due to rain until yesterday morning when they finally began. In the morning, one group played singles, and another in the afternoon. Unexpectedly, both Japanese groups were completely defeated. If the Philippines can win one of the remaining three singles groups, they will win the championship. Cavia's 3-1 victory over Itada shows his improvement.

Singles 254

(Dentsu, Manila, 20th) The Japan-Philippines tennis singles match between Yamada and Cavia started fiercely. The first set was tied three times, but Cavia won. In the second set, Yamada fought back and turned defeat into victory. The third set was tied at 5-5. After further play, Yamada lost again. In the fourth set, Yamada was expected to retaliate, but he failed, losing 6-1. The Philippines won 3-1.

Cavia (Philippines) (9-7, 4-6, 7-5, 6-1) Keigo Yamada (Japan)

Doubles 255

(Dentsu, Manila, 20th) The Japan-Philippines tennis doubles match, postponed to today due to rain, was held at 2 PM today. The Philippine team was represented by T. Zamora, and the Japanese team by Sato and Yamagishi. The Japanese team had the initial advantage, winning the first set. The Philippine team then turned defeat into victory, winning the second and third sets. The Japanese team fought back, winning the fourth set to tie the match. After further play, the Philippine team finally won the final fifth set 6-4.

T. Zamora (Philippines) (2-6, 6-2, 6-1, 3-6, 6-4) Sato and Yamagishi (Japan)

Another Singles Match Incomplete 256

(Dentsu News Agency, Manila, 20th)

In the Japan-Philippines tennis singles match between Taro Sato and Aragon, Japan had previously lost twice, so Sato was determined to fight hard to save Japan's reputation. He started very cautiously. He easily won the first set 6-1. In the second set, Aragon's spirits rose, and the battle was fierce, reaching 5-5 and 6-6. Sato won the second set. In the third set, Aragon's momentum was strong, and he worked hard to reverse the trend. He won 8-6 this time. By then, it was already dark, and it was difficult to continue the game, so it was decided to continue the match tomorrow morning. Today's result is Sato 2-1, Japan ahead.

Sato (Japan) (6-2, 8-6, 6-8) Aragon (Philippines)

Amidst the Enthusiastic Atmosphere of Sports Meets, Physical Education Instructors Should Read Physical Education Books 262

In recent years, our country, both government and public, have been promoting physical education with all their might. Recently, under the pressure of strong neighbors, it has become even more enthusiastic, hoping to revive the nation. However, promoting physical education cannot be accomplished by empty talk, nor can it be achieved by simply holding a few sports meets. We should first earnestly study the principles of physical education and competitive training methods to make rapid progress and achieve satisfactory results. More than one hundred physical education experts across the country have jointly written "Physical Education Books," which cover all aspects of physical education principles, administration, history, architecture, gymnastics, track and field, swimming, ball games, dance, etc. It is published by the Shanghai Diligent Bookstore and is well-known throughout the country. Recently, according to the primary school curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry of Education, they jointly wrote "Primary School Physical Education Teaching Materials," a total of 25 volumes. With this set of the latest teaching materials, primary school physical education teachers can teach students in lower, middle, and upper grades for six years. In addition, "Diligent Physical Education Monthly" is China's only regular physical education publication, with rich text and illustrations, emphasizing both theory and technology. Special issues on primary and secondary school physical education are popular throughout the country. The eighth issue is "The 10th Far Eastern Games Special Issue, Volume 1," which has already been published. The ninth issue is the Far Eastern Games Special Issue, Volume 2, which is an essential monthly magazine for physical education instructors, athletes, and school libraries. The whole year of twelve issues is sold for only two yuan, with no domestic postage. Overseas add two yuan and two jiao.

Educational News

Jiangxi Provincial Department of Education to Run a Summer School in Lushan 273

Lushan is a scenic area famous throughout history, with lush forests and beautiful springs, and a temperate climate, making it an excellent place to escape the summer heat. During the height of summer and early autumn, thousands of Chinese and foreign people bring their families to visit. In light of this, the Jiangxi Provincial Department of Education has specifically obtained approval from the provincial government to establish a summer tutorial school in Guling this summer, so that male and female students can benefit from learning and cultivation amidst waterfalls and clouds. It is reported that the post of school principal will be concurrently held by the Director of the Department of Education, Cheng Shi. Xia Jiahong has been hired as the director of academic affairs. Mr. Xia has studied in the United States for many years and is talented and knowledgeable. The teachers in each subject are all experienced and specialized. The facilities are complete and the scale is grand. Internally, it is divided into middle school, elementary school, and kindergarten, piano classes. The subjects include Chinese, English, mathematics, music, and physical education. The period of study is from July 4th to September the blankth. The registration period is from today to July 5th. Lushan has always been a famous ancient area for learning, and with this school, it will not allow the Deer Cave Academy and the White Stone Academy to monopolize the beauty of the past.

Jiangsu Province Middle School Enrollment Methods 274

Class Size Limited to Forty to Fifty Students

All Methods of Recommendation and Direct Enrollment Are Abolished

Zhenjiang Correspondence. The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education has formulated the Provisional Measures for Enrollment in Provincial Secondary Schools for the 23rd academic year, which are recorded below: (Article 1) New students in senior high schools and junior high schools, in addition to recruiting graduates from junior high schools and elementary schools, may also recruit those with equivalent academic qualifications, but this shall not exceed 10% of the total enrollment. (Note) Equivalent academic qualifications refer to a level in all subjects equivalent to that of graduates from elementary schools or junior high schools. (Article 2) New students in normal schools and simplified rural normal schools shall recruit graduates from junior high schools and elementary schools. (Article 3) Senior and junior vocational school new students, in addition to recruiting graduates from junior high schools and elementary schools, may also recruit those with a corresponding level, but this shall not exceed 2% of the total enrollment. (Note) Corresponding level refers to those who have not formally graduated from elementary or junior high school, but who have a corresponding level of knowledge in subjects related to their chosen profession. (Article 4) The class size shall be 40 to 50 students for senior and junior high schools, 45 students for normal schools, and 15 to 40 students for senior and junior vocational schools. (Article 5) Enrollment of new students in senior high schools, junior high schools, girls' normal schools, simplified rural normal schools, senior and junior vocational schools is not limited to regions. Normal schools should enroll students from counties within the normal school district. The allocation of quotas for each district county is as follows: District 1, Zhenjiang Normal School District, includes the eleven counties of Zhenjiang, Danyang, Jiangning, Jiangpu, Jurong, Liuhe, Gaochun, Lishui, Yangzhou, Jiangdu, and Yizheng, with four people from each county, and one remaining place. District 2, Wuxi Normal School District, includes the ten counties of Wuxi, Wujin, Yixing, Liyang, Jiangyin, Jingjiang, Jintan, Wuxian, Wujiang, and Changshu, with four people from each county, and five remaining places. District 3, Taicang Normal School District, includes the twelve counties of Taicang, Kunshan, Jiading, Shanghai, Songjiang, Nanhui, Qingpu, Fengxian, Jinshan, Chuansha, Baoshan, and Chongming, with three people from each county, and nine remaining places. District 4, Huaiyin Normal School District, includes the nine counties of Huaiyin, Huaian, Siyang, Lianshui, Shuyang, Suqian, Gaoyou, Baoying, and Funing, with five people from each county. District 5,

Donghai Normal School District includes the ten counties of Donghai, Tongshan, Feng, Pei, Xiao, Dangshan, Pi, Suining, Guanyun, and Ganyu, with four people from each county, and five remaining places. District 6, Rugao Normal School District, includes the nine counties of Rugao, Nantong, Taixing, Dongtai, Taixian, Xinghua, Yancheng, Haimen, and Qidong, with five people from each county. The remaining places in each district will still be filled by selecting the best candidates from each county within the district. If the quota for each county is not met, it may be supplemented by selecting the best candidates from other counties within the district. (Article 6) The number of students in normal schools and simplified rural normal schools is limited to students from this province. Non-local students who audit courses shall pay the corresponding fees according to regulations. (Article 7) New students in provincial secondary schools shall not be admitted without an entrance examination. All previous methods of recommendation and direct enrollment are hereby abolished. (Article 8) Entrance examinations shall be conducted in accordance with the Provisional Measures for Entrance Examinations promulgated by the Department of Education. (Article 9) Middle schools and normal schools recruiting transfer students must have transfer certificates and transcripts with corresponding academic terms from other middle schools or normal schools. Senior and junior vocational schools must have transfer certificates and transcripts with corresponding academic terms and majors. After review and verification, those who pass the grade placement examination may be admitted. (Article 10) Schools shall not recruit transfer students into the third grade, nor shall they issue transfer certificates. (Article 11) Graduates from private middle schools and elementary schools that have not been approved for establishment shall not be admitted as new students or transfer students. (Article 12) The registration fee shall be limited to one yuan per person. (Article 13) Examination questions and admission results shall be reported to the Department of Education for record within one month. (Article 14) Statistics on entrance examinations for each school shall be reported in the prescribed format within one month, with the statistical table attached (omitted). (Article 15) These measures shall be promulgated and implemented by the Department of Education.

Tongji University's 27th Anniversary Celebration 275

Today is the 27th anniversary of National Tongji University. The university held a grand celebration ceremony. The meeting was held in the university's auditorium starting at 9:00 AM, with many dignitaries present, which can be called a grand event. After the ceremony, President Weng Zhilong reported on the general situation of the university, saying that the graduates of the university over the past 27 years have gained considerable reputation in society. In the past four years, the number of students has increased from 548 to 863, and there is still a regret that the supply cannot meet the demand. As for the economic aspect, although there has been an increase every year, it is still not very generous due to the huge expenses of adding senior vocational schools, higher surveying departments, affiliated middle schools, two colleges of public health research institutes, and sending students to study abroad. Regarding the development of undertakings, the medical school, in addition to adding a public health lectureship and cooperating with hospitals in Changzhou, Jintan, and Wuxi, is preparing to add a hospital, because the Baolong Hospital is not enough to accommodate the increasing number of interns. In addition to adding a higher surveying department this year, the College of Engineering is preparing to cooperate with the Ministry of Communications to add shipbuilding, aircraft, and mechanical engineering departments to meet the needs of the country. As for the equipment aspect, the school buildings have been repaired completely after being destroyed by the January 28th Incident. However, the German donation of materials for factories and research institutes is very appreciated. In addition, the library and hydraulic research institute have been completed, but the swimming pool is still under construction. President Weng finally expressed his gratitude to the government authorities and the German consul for their various assistance to the school. After the president's report, representatives from the Party Committee gave speeches. Guests such as Cai Jimin, President of the Academia Sinica, Duan Xipeng, Vice Minister of Education, the German Consul General, representatives from the German Alumni Association and the Tongji Alumni Association, and Huang Boqiao all gave speeches successively, with many words of encouragement, and congratulated President Weng for his talent. Then, the unveiling ceremony of the memorial碑 for the late Professor Shi Lou'na, Dean of the College of Engineering, and Professor Oteman, Dean of the Affiliated Middle School, was held. Huang Boqiao, Director of the Two-Road Railway Bureau, and Shen Junyi, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Public Works Bureau, unveiled the monument with solemnity. After the ceremony and photography, President Weng led the guests to visit the research institutes and test sites of various departments. It is said that the guests praised them repeatedly.
