Free Talk

Famous Principles 286

— Hengsha

There is no lack of various great principles in the world, which sound pleasant, make beautiful articles, and are quite impressive when acted upon, but we know that they are not desirable.

Let's take Buddhist principles as an example. To persuade people to do good and be compassionate, aren't the teachings themselves very healthy? Generals' books may be engraved with "Buddhist disciple"; social scoundrels may also call themselves "lay Buddhists"; after scraping the land and taking concubines, they donate some money to repair Buddhist temples and print Buddhist scriptures, and thus become old-fashioned gentlemen. If you listen to wild foxes talking about Chan Buddhist principles, you feel that their principles are super-super, forgetting that they are wild foxes. Lu You has a poem that says: "Silks and embroideries show off women's work, poets cry poor here," this is what it means.

That principle, Zhuangzi already had the "Opening Coffers" chapter, there is no need to explain it. Stealing with both benevolence and righteousness, becoming a weapon to protect oneself, what method can be thought of? Go ask the bureaucrats, please sit down, don't be busy, he can explain it clearly. Western principles, picked up at random, say one thing in a flowery way; fighting for territory, it's to relieve the suffering of the people! Snatching jobs, it's to be unwilling to give way! If things go wrong, it's because China has no talent! Even to the point of a complete defeat, it's to retreat to advance, it's also the principle in the Book of Changes!

Therefore, the common people have to be silent and retreat.

But sometimes a rich man suddenly becomes poor, or a powerful person suddenly collapses, then the true face is revealed, neither crying nor laughing, at this time benevolence and morality are not working. Even if Buddhism says that everything is empty, it is not working, there is nothing to comfort them, so Zhuangzi also wrote the "Robber Zhi" chapter in addition to the "Opening Coffers" chapter, maybe it was fabricated by later generations, but that thinking is roughly consistent.

However, logic also has times of exhaustion, the principles of the Book of Changes are finally incomplete, the principles of principles have been occupied, the world still needs to change, because the common people often have no reason to talk about but are really persistent in unspeakable reasons. If the Japanese once swallowed China, we undoubtedly, the principles will go to that side again.

But this is still not terrible, the principle of no reason will break the principle of reason, cheating and cheating through, it is not surprising. Were the Manchus not strict in ruling the Han people in the Qing Dynasty, did not the civil and military achievements reach the extreme, but in the end there was the Republic of China, why?

Reminiscences 287

— Gao Bi

— Written for the Third Anniversary of the Death of My Late Friend Chen Hangshu —

(I) On a breezy early summer evening, the sun was already hanging on the treetops, patches of wandering clouds were rolling and rippling in the sky. I, harboring a slight feeling of sadness, leaned against the window alone, lost in thought. After many memories of past reunions and separations, joys and sorrows flashed through my mind, I suddenly remembered Chen Hangshu, who passed away in France three years ago -- today happens to be the exact third anniversary -- and I suddenly felt a heavy oppression in my heart. He was an absolutely transcendent typical youth. He embodied all the virtues of mankind: he possessed unparalleled intelligence, he harbored profound cultivation, he had keen talent and exquisite skills, he could use his special intellect to observe the changes of all things, he could exert his sharp insights to cope with the arrival of all difficulties, he was not arrogant, not rigid, not cunning, not mean, always maintaining a gentle attitude to give anyone a good impression. Once we experienced his elegant style, lingering emotions, and graceful conversation, we would all unconsciously fall for him. However, it was precisely because he was too smart, too thoughtful, that he could thoroughly understand others but could not understand himself; he could use his inspiration to give comfort to others but could not get his own comfort from others. In this way, he could not avoid embarking on the road of melancholy. At the same time, he focused too much on the pursuit of learning, neglecting the care of his body, and finally died of intestinal tuberculosis before his doctoral thesis was even drafted. His death shook a part of scholars at home and abroad. Undoubtedly, this is a pity for talent, not just a private mourning. Regarding his entire learning and thought, someone should write a biography for him, so I won't go into details now. What I am constantly thinking about is some emotional fragments and connections, which I cannot help but express in writing. I was the one who knew him since he was a child. Among the few of us, he was always regarded as a little brother; however, his bright and radiant light was often regarded by us as a bright lamp in a dark room, and his warmth towards us was like adding a steam heater to a cold cellar. Now, the cold air has not dissipated, the heater has been removed first, the night is still dark, and the aura is suddenly gone. How can we not be devastated and heartbroken!

(II)

My first meeting with Hangshu was probably in the early years of the Republic of China. At that time, his fourth brother, Shuliang, and I were studying at the local county high school. One day, when school was dismissed, I found a child of about seven or eight years old wandering in the corridor outside the student dormitory. His delicate eyebrows, rosy cheeks, and the gentle smile that he occasionally revealed attracted the attention of many students. Later, I learned that he was Shuliang's younger brother who had come from the countryside to visit his brother, and everyone happily went to talk to him. Originally, we wanted to tease him, but unexpectedly, his conversation was very civilized and organized, unlike what a seven or eight-year-old child could say; and between questions and answers, his attitude was as generous as an adult, which naturally surprised us -- at that time, the general school age of primary school students seemed to be higher than it is now, so our classmates were mostly around fourteen or fifteen years old and could understand some worldly affairs. From that time on, he left me with an indelible impression.

(III)

He was only fourteen years old when he entered middle school, and his excellent grades won unanimous praise from the entire school. Not only did he always win first place in every exam, but he also showed many contributions outside of schoolwork. He had special ambitions, but he didn't often talk about them casually with others. He was not like ordinary "excellent" students who studied for exams; he liked to find knowledge outside of textbooks to integrate his consistent pursuits. He disdained the high or low scores on test papers, but only suffered from the inability to satisfy himself. For always being at the top of the list, he certainly didn't have any "smugness"; on the contrary, he thought that others were looking down on him too much for complimenting him based on the list. In order to avoid the concentration of other people's attention, he tried his best to learn to be casual, doing some naughty things, and even violated the school rules and was punished; he just smiled. He was so friendly and amiable to his classmates that he maintained a considerable friendship with almost everyone, and his words were so tactful and relaxed that almost every sentence could touch the hearts of others. He was really an exquisite and ingenious person, he was really a little elf!

(IV)

My close association with him began after the May Fourth Movement. At that time, we ran a small publication; in addition to him and me, there were also Hu Zhongchi and Mao Wuzhi. Editing, proofreading, printing, and distribution were almost all handled by us. We were extremely busy, but under mutual coordination, the work was very organized. In particular, Hangshu unfolded his skillful and impeccable skills, giving us a very enthusiastic interest. Even someone like me, who has always been lazy, was happy to engage in it under his encouragement and supervision. The writings in the publication were just some casual feelings published by us, but he often had novel ideas and fluent writing, which could be thought-provoking. I still remember that once he said in his random notes:

'...Occasionally walking in the suburbs, I feel that this natural beauty is really reluctant to give up. I can't help but think: if I were isolated from the world, quietly enjoying the pleasure of natural beauty, that would be a truly joyful and meaningful life! Because of this thought, I feel that the reason why we are human is simply because we are attracted by the joy in front and forced by the misery of death behind, so we go all out to be human, which shows that life is indeed manipulated by emotions.'

'So my judgment is: a life of emotion is active, a life of reason is passive, a life of emotion is a transcendent way, and a life of reason is an worldly way; according to biology, the instinct of life originates from the need for self-preservation, and in our current situation, we can only be satisfied with the passive worldly way.'

Such an admirer of transcendence coming from a fifteen or sixteen-year-old youth would surprise anyone. Cuchi once said generously: 'This little brother is really beyond the reach of our group of brothers!' This sentence was unanimously recognized at the time.

The distribution of the publication was relatively difficult. The motivation for us to run this publication was to arouse the patriotic enthusiasm of the citizens, and of course we hoped to have many readers; however, there was no funding, and printing paper cost money, so it was difficult to send it out universally. We had to start from selling it. Because there were so few subscribers, we had to brave the scorching sun, carrying the crystal of our heart's blood, and go to the streets to 'peddle' door to door. This was naturally unfamiliar to us, but we had to reluctantly engage in it. As a result of 'peddling' separately, the number of copies sold by us was often less than that sold by Hangshu, because his tactful expression easily won the sympathy of the citizens -- I often didn't sell even one copy. But later, he found that most citizens threw it away casually after buying our publication. He became very unhappy and said angrily to us: 'We have spent so much effort and energy without getting any reward, it's like receiving their alms, what's the point!' As a result of the discussion, our publication finally stopped there.

Why Do We Throw Rice at the Bride and Groom? 288

— Cao Juren

In Zheng Zhenduo's translation of "Introduction to Folklore," there is a section explaining "Why do we throw rice at the bride and groom?" 'Some will say this is a blessing; rice is a symbol of abundance. The Chinese also perform the same ceremony with rice (the hostess throws rice on the bride's head as she enters her future home). Rice is a symbol of abundance.' In my opinion, this explanation is somewhat incorrect, regardless of the customs of the ancient ethnic groups of Celebes, India, and certain parts of England.

In our country's custom, when the bride steps out of the sedan chair, what is thrown on her is not only rice, but also tea leaves, shredded red paper, and the like. The meaning is not to bless, but to exorcise evil. The virginity of a virgin is seen as very mysterious in feudal society, and it is felt that demons are constantly taking the opportunity to cause trouble; even during this grand ceremony, the demons are desperately making a final disturbance. The groom's head is covered with a red scarf, and the sedan chair door is hung with rice stalks. The rice stalks are tied with objects such as a ten-thousand-year calendar, a copper mirror, and a tailor's ruler, forming a Bagua array to prevent demons from entering. As soon as the bride gets out of the sedan chair, tea leaves and rice are quickly sprinkled on her to make the demons stay away, so as to complete the perfect merit. The use of tea leaves and rice has the same meaning in ordinary times for driving away evil spirits and sending away stars for patients.

Why do tea leaves and rice have the effect of driving away evil spirits? Humans believe that things that maintain life have supreme divine power. Tea leaves quench thirst, and rice fills the stomach. Getting them means life, and losing them means death. Needless to say, they are the most powerful things in the world. By analogy, things like scales, rulers, rice sieves, and calendars, which are directly or indirectly related to maintaining life, become our guards. We cannot see or hear demons and evil spirits, so we ask these powerful guards to deal with them. The true meaning of sprinkling rice should be explained this way.

There is another kind of ritual text for blessing customs in marriage. On the day the bride is about to marry, from bathing, dressing, combing her hair, and wearing flowers, the elderly and senior relatives will recite blessings for her. Every time she does something, there is a blessing. From the bride's own door to the sedan chair door, her feet do not touch the ground. A rice bag is placed on the ground, passed on from person to person, called passing on the lineage. The curtains, quilts, and clothes in the room are all deeply dyed blue, wishing them love. On the wedding day, gifts are given to guests, such as melon seeds and peanuts, wishing for the continuation of their descendants.

These blessing rituals are completely separate from sprinkling tea leaves and rice, and they are not related or confused.

Someone asked: 'Bismarck once said, "People in the tropics worship the sun because the sun is dangerous and hot in the tropics; the Teutons also worship lightning for similar reasons. In these matters, human nature is revealed, which is the same as dogs, who love and respect those they fear." Isn't his explanation extremely accurate?' We should agree with his statement that worshiping the sun, fire, snakes, and reproductive worship are all simple materialist views that can be said to be the origin of theism. Believing that tea leaves and rice can drive away evil spirits has the same origin in psychology.

That is my explanation.

Stimulation 289

— Sheng Fu

Behaviorists explain behavior with stimulation, saying, "All behavior is based on stimulation, but the repetition of stimulation will also reduce its intensity, until in the end, it will be so weak that it is almost numb. If the same stimulation is repeated, one will not even feel it at all." This is indeed close to the truth.

Love is a more complex stimulation. Some say that marriage is the tomb of love, which is probably because the stimulation of love becomes nearly saturated after marriage. If no new stimulation occurs, it is difficult for the old stimulation to evoke the old love.

Terror is also a non-simple stimulus. But the repetition of terror can also numb people and no longer be terror. As the saying goes: "Courage is frightened." It is not unreasonable. When young, adults often use monsters and tigers to scare them. At first, they are indeed a little afraid, but after hearing about them for a long time, they no longer believe them. A person who travels at night will inevitably be worried at first, seeing gods and ghosts. People who are accustomed to walking at night have more stimulation and find night travel more interesting.

The first time I saw a beheading, I felt it was a bit scary. I ran away before I really saw it clearly. Later, because I had the opportunity to see beheadings every day, it became commonplace. When my own friend was killed, I could even help others identify the body from the corpse pile, which was really unexpected before.

In short, the repetition of stimulation can change its nature, which is a truth. Therefore, mothers who use terror tactics to scare their children, although it can be used for a while, will eventually make the children bolder and give birth to a contemptuous and untrustworthy mood for the elders.

Eugenie (5) 290

— Bai Wei

On the first day in Berlin, it was drizzling slightly. In the morning, they visited several museums for a while. Eugenie felt a little unwell, so she stayed in the hotel in the afternoon.

'I feel a bit strange. Shall we go visit a doctor?' Eugenie said.

'Okay, let's go.'

They found a doctor on Kant Street. Eugenie spoke in German for a while. The doctor nodded frequently, but Xuan didn't understand a word. Then, Eugenie was led to the inner room and came out after a few minutes. Eugenie asked Xuan to pay the consultation fee, and they returned to the hotel.

'Darling, I'm pregnant!' Eugenie said with a mischievous expression as soon as she entered the room.

'Really?' This was a bolt from the blue for Xuan.

'Of course it's true, the doctor just confirmed it.' She sat down next to Xuan, and Xuan put his arms around her waist. She said coquettishly: 'When I was preparing for the exam, you kept asking me... I was lazy, I skipped those preventive measures. My body has been a little different for the past half a month; it turned out to be this!'

'Darling, did you ask about the methods of termination?' Xuan asked worriedly.

'What do you ask that for?'

'Aren't you going to terminate this little life that came wrong? This little life that we can't keep!'

'Why do you say such things? To be honest, I'm happy about it! Didn't you say that our love doesn't have any fitting souvenirs? Now, isn't the souvenir coming on its own? Is there any more fitting souvenir than this? Now you're saying we can't keep it!'

'It can be kept... You have to sacrifice your family and go back to Paris with me! That way, we can keep this little life!'

'Darling, forgive me: on this point, my opinion is different from yours again. Now I'm going home. First, this fait accompli will facilitate our marriage; second, my mother can take care of me and our child. Do you think you can understand women's affairs?'

'As you said before, since your mother is so proud, how can she tolerate her unmarried daughter giving birth to a child?'

'These are two different things! The factors involved are completely different. It's like my giving birth and marrying you. The attitude of the church towards these two things is completely different. I have better ways to deal with my family. — In short, I don't want to sacrifice the crystallization of our love! I still want to go home. Next March or April, after I give birth, I will take the earliest opportunity to bring the child to Paris to find you. Don't you like it?'

'I like it,' Xuan replied helplessly. He knew Eugenie's stubborn temper; he understood the maternal love in a woman's nature; he was convinced of women's innate ability to deal with such difficulties, and he had nothing else to say. He thought about it from the opposite perspective: maybe because of this new life, the current separation won't be forever! With this bridge, Eugenie can belong to him forever! He felt at ease again.

They toured Berlin for a few more days as if on a honeymoon, and Eugenie prepared to take the train south. The first night, they told each other countless words and made countless vows! The next day, this eternally elegant and graceful girl waved goodbye with a bitter smile in the train window and was taken away by the train! Xuan's tears fell like strings.

Hurriedly leaving Berlin, that sad place, Xuan returned to Paris alone. Recalling this beautiful dream of the past two years, he was immersed in an unnamed melancholy and anxiety! Every night, his dream soul struggled to follow the flow of the Danube eastward!

May the God of Love bless the holy Eugenie and the little life she is carrying! (End)

Page 18

Economic Special Issue Published Every Sunday Issue 73

Comments on the National Financial Conference Amidst the Noise

Two Proposals by the Ministry of Finance for Reorganizing Land Tax 291

— Liu Zhipan

Recently, the Ministry of Finance convened a national financial conference, which opened today in Beijing. Financial authorities from various provinces were summoned to discuss practical and important issues such as the reorganization of land tax, the abolition of exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies, and the preparation of local budgets. It is reported that this conference will particularly emphasize the discussion of reorganizing land tax. The Ministry of Finance has already drafted two proposals and, before submitting them to the conference, seeks the opinions of authorities and local figures in various provinces, hoping to gather diverse perspectives. This spirit of humility and dedication to governance is truly admirable. Having examined county finances for many years, I have some understanding of the long-standing abuses in land tax. After reading the two proposals of the Ministry of Finance on reorganizing land tax, I deeply feel that they address the current malpractices and are concise and to the point. According to the Ministry of Finance, the two proposals to be submitted to the conference are: one is a plan to conduct land reporting, and the other is a strategy to alleviate surcharges in order to revitalize the rural economy. In addition to providing detailed measures, both proposals analyze in detail the current abuses in land tax and the causes of rural economic bankruptcy. The original text of these two proposals is recorded at the beginning of this article for reference:

Proposal (1)

Proposal to Conduct Land Reporting Prior to Reorganizing Land Tax to Eliminate Long-Standing Abuses and Enrich Tax Revenue, Requesting Public Decision

It is found that among our country's tax systems, land tax is the most ancient, and its long-standing abuses are also the most profound. Over the past centuries, through various changes and reforms, the categories have become numerous and complicated, the tax rates are uneven, and differ from province to province and even from county to county. Currently, most of the cadastral registers no longer exist, and the grain household registers are also incomplete. The collection of land tax in each county relies solely on books secretly kept by clerks. This accumulated habit has led to numerous abuses, resulting in discrepancies between land and tax, or land without tax, and tax without land. Moreover, there are many cases of garrison lands, mountain wetlands, and urban residential lands that were not registered and taxed in the past due to special reasons. As a result, practices such as concealment, fictitious transfers, and embezzlement have arisen one after another. What the people pay cannot fully go to the public, and the government's revenue is declining daily. The debt is not with the people, and the revenue does not enter the government. Speaking of fundamental reorganization methods, the solution lies in conducting a comprehensive land survey and reforming to collect land value tax. However, considering the current national situation, popular sentiment, talent, and economy, it is not feasible to achieve results in a short time. Currently, to reorganize land tax, the only option is to treat the symptoms urgently. The best way to treat the symptoms is to conduct land reporting first, requiring landowners to report and register their household names, land locations, boundaries, area, and tax amount themselves, and provide them with certificates. Each county can then use this information to compile a more accurate and complete formal tax register. Those with discrepancies between land and tax can be corrected accordingly, those with land but no tax can be supplemented, and those with tax but no land can also be deleted. Furthermore, the original complex tax rates can also be separately reduced and merged, so that tax amounts are fair and not excessively heavy or light. With this preliminary work in place, there will be a basis for future investigation. In the future, implementing fundamental solutions such as comprehensive land surveys or land value assessments will be easier to promote. Currently, governments in various provinces also generally know that there is a significant difference between the amount of land and the amount of tax. However, their methods of investigation are all carried out exclusively by dispatched officials. The local interests and public concerns are often not taken into consideration, so they often fail to achieve results. Or, due to improper use of personnel, turmoil arises. This is due to poor planning and not because the matter is infeasible. To correct this, the only way is to find ways to make the people have a vested interest in land reporting, then things will be easier to do, and the effect will be easier to see. The following is a draft outline of measures:

(A) Provincial governments should formulate detailed rules for land reporting based on local conditions. Counties should select impartial gentry and legal representatives to organize land survey agencies to persuade people to engage in land reporting, so that the government can compile tax registers and revise tax laws.

(B) The central government should clearly stipulate that the increased tax revenue from this reporting will be retained to fund local expenses and used to offset surcharges as an incentive.

(C) All those who have land but no tax or more land than tax and report within the time limit will be allowed to supplement their tax. Those who conceal and fail to report will be investigated and severely punished or their concealed land will be confiscated. All fines and confiscated land will be divided to be used for public welfare needs in the county and district, and to reward informants.

(D) Those who report on time or delay their reporting within the extended time limit will be allowed to have their tax amount reduced or increased appropriately to show rewards and punishments. Land that is not reported will be deemed to have lost its property rights. Transfers, mortgages, and inheritance will be valid only with the land reporting certificate.

(E) Government officials who handle the reporting and check the reported land, and are deemed to have achieved excellent results, will be rewarded accordingly.

(F) The county should select the original bookkeepers and appoint them as paid officials, and provide them with real protection, ordering them to fully disclose the original tax registers for verification.

(G) Provincial governments should, in imitation of the registration methods of architects and accountants, formulate special regulations to examine and select personnel with surveying knowledge or experience, issue them licenses, and allow them to carry out surveying businesses in various counties, so that people can entrust them to survey their land at any time.

The above-proposed measures are only the major points of the easy-to-implement reorganization of land tax. The only goal is for the measures to be effective, and I dare not discuss profound theories. As for all the laws and regulations and implementation procedures, the central government and the provinces should carefully consider local conditions and handle them separately. Whether they are appropriate, I hereby request a public decision.

Proposal (2)

Proposal to Reduce Land Tax Surcharges to Revitalize the Rural Economy and Relieve the People's Hardship, Requesting Public Decision

It is found that in various provinces, land tax, with the exception of a few that have no surcharges, mostly have surcharges exceeding the original tax. Although the numbers are different, the people's ability to bear it is the same. Since the abolition of likin, all kinds of local undertakings have been establishing various items under the land tax, collecting surcharges along with the original tax. Among them, there is no lack of necessary expenses, but excessive spending and over-collection are also common, and the arbitrary apportionments in various rural districts are even worse. The merchants who were formerly afflicted by likin are now afflicted by agricultural surcharges. Currently, agricultural surcharges exceed the original tax by more than twenty times in some cases. At a time when the rural economy is bankrupt and the people are extremely distressed, if no urgent efforts are made to save the situation, the situation will develop further, the people's hardship will deepen, and communist bandits will be able to take advantage of this to incite the public. The hidden worries for the future are unbearable to imagine. Therefore, agricultural surcharges should be greatly reduced based on the ability of the people to bear them. However, in order to effectively reduce agricultural surcharges, the county's local finances must first be incorporated into the overall scope, so that agricultural surcharges and their uses are listed by district and township and reported to the county, and the county government verifies and reports to the province. Then, the true picture of the county's local revenue and expenditure can be clarified, and there will be a way to determine which surcharges should be immediately abolished, which should be temporarily postponed, which should be reduced, and which should be suspended within a time limit. After the reduction, if it is necessary to offset the reduction, there will also be an accurate amount to verify. Therefore, determining the county's local budget is the only way to limit surcharges. The following is a draft outline of measures:

(A) Determine the county's local financial budget, and all regular and temporary revenues and expenditures of the entire county, whether collected and disbursed by county government agencies or district and township offices, should be included in the estimates. After being reviewed by the county, it should be reported to the provincial government for strict review.

(B) The provincial government's review of the county's local budget should be limited to the total amount of agricultural surcharges not exceeding the original tax. If the approved county business expenses included in the budget are insufficient due to the reduction of surcharges, in addition to using the increased land tax from land reporting to make up for it, it can apply to the provincial government for approval to allocate funds for subsidies. If the provincial budget is insufficient, it can also apply to the central government for verification and special approval for assistance.

(C) All county local financial revenues and expenditures, whether county funds or district funds, should be uniformly reviewed and publicly announced by the county financial authorities, and all legal entities should be allowed to check the accounts at any time.

(D) After the county budget is finalized and announced, any revenues and expenditures outside the budget that have not been approved by the provincial government in advance should be severely punished in accordance with the punishment regulations established by the province.

The above-proposed measures are to enable the county to have a definite budget, to prevent arbitrary levies and excessive spending, so that surcharges can be effectively reduced, relieving the people's pain, and thus revitalizing the countryside and curbing the rise of chaos. Whether they are appropriate, I hereby request a public decision.

From the original text of the above two proposals, the reader should know the entire plan of the Ministry of Finance for reorganizing land tax. The former proposal regards conducting land reporting as a prerequisite for reorganizing land tax, while the latter proposal regards reducing the burden and revitalizing the countryside as the most urgent and greatest task at present. Based on my personal observations, I would like to comment on the contents of these two proposals separately for the reference of the attendees of the National Financial Conference:

(A) Regarding the Land Reporting Proposal:

(1) Should land reporting be uniformly conducted first to reorganize land tax?

It is true that our country's land tax urgently needs reorganization, and this is known to everyone. However, how to reorganize it is a matter of debate and there is no consensus. Generally speaking, the most fundamental solution is a comprehensive land survey, while the best way to treat the symptoms is to check and compile registers of grain tax. Land reporting is only one of the methods to check and compile the registers of grain tax. However, considering the local conditions, the provinces are different from each other, and the counties are different from each other. Therefore, the methods of checking and compiling maps and registers cannot be forced to fit everyone, and one cannot be forced to be the same. There are counties that should conduct land reporting; there are counties that should conduct land surveys; and there are counties that only need to conduct household name corrections because the bottom registers of tax collection have long been recovered. Since the conditions of each county are different, the method should be the responsibility of the provincial governments to consider the conditions of each county and separately determine the reorganization method. Facts should not be obliterated, and land reporting should not be uniformly conducted first. According to the conditions of various counties in Jiangsu, the counties of Jiangning, Jiangyin, Yixing, and Liyang have the deepest long-standing abuses in land tax and should conduct land reporting. However, for counties in Jiangnan with lighter abuses in land tax, and for various counties in Jiangbei, because their conditions are different, whether land reporting should be conducted uniformly is a matter to be carefully considered. For example, in various counties in Jiangbei, several counties have requested that land tax be investigated at the same time as the household registration survey, which is very economical in terms of manpower and financial resources, and is indeed easy to implement and a win-win situation. Also, in Jiangnan, such as Wu County, the bottom registers of tax collection have been recovered, and the history of the transfer and assignment of property rights of all owners is recorded in great detail. If the names and addresses of the owners can be corrected, then this register will be more complete than the land reporting register, because it is difficult to investigate and report in detail and completely the history of previous property rights transfers in the land reporting register. Some may say that the registers of tax collection are only registers of the original tax amount, and there is still no way to find out about concealed, tax-free land. This is indeed a point worth considering. I believe that investigating and squeezing out concealed grain tax cannot be achieved by reporting, and cannot be accomplished without a comprehensive land survey. Land reporting, for investigating and squeezing out concealed grain tax, is possible but not certain. Since people are allowed to report themselves, there are those who over-report and those who under-report. Considering human nature, the former are few and the latter are many. Therefore, with the amount of over-reporting and under-reporting offsetting each other, the amount that can be newly added is still likely to be very little. For the present plan, for counties with the deepest abuses in land tax, land investigation and reporting should be conducted. On the one hand, the government should supervise the various districts, townships, and towns to handle land reporting; on the other hand, the land administration agencies and finance departments of various provinces should closely cooperate to conduct land surveys. Making reporting and surveying go hand in hand can both make up for the shortcomings of reporting and avoid the complexity of future comprehensive land surveys. Then, a simple comprehensive land survey has been carried out, and a detailed cadastral register has been obtained, which is a very good and beautiful thing. Currently, the plan for land survey in Jiangsu Province has been re-established, and it is already quite similar to the non-conforming claims. As for other counties with complete registers, and counties that have already completed land surveys in the former Qing Dynasty, there is no need to conduct land investigation and reporting, only the system of bow rulers for tax collection and land tax collection needs to be rectified. (2) Criticism of the various measures proposed in the proposal

(1) For the general outline of measures in Part A, please consider the following points: 1. The general outline of this plan applies to counties that conduct land investigation and reporting; it does not apply to counties that do not need to conduct land investigation and reporting.

2. The key to land investigation and reporting is to actually implement it. The provincial governments should carefully select county magistrates in various counties to be responsible for its real implementation. It does not seem necessary to uniformly organize land survey agencies.

3. The method of land tax investigation should not be carried out exclusively by dispatched officials; however, even with strong persuasion, it may be difficult to achieve real results if people report themselves. Therefore, in addition to reporting on the one hand, investigation should be carried out at the same time.

4. This item should be revised as follows:

"Provincial governments should consider the local conditions and conduct land investigation and reporting in various counties, formulate detailed rules, select impartial gentry and legal representatives to participate, and supervise the various district and township heads to guide the people to engage in land reporting, and also jointly assign surveying personnel to visit and survey households at any time in cooperation with the provincial and county land administration agencies."

(2) For Part B, please consider the following points:

1. Whether land reporting can actually increase the tax amount is still a question. It is enough to hope that the previously unreal false registers can be turned into reliable and consistent registers with the original amount. If you want to produce a huge amount of additional land, it cannot be accomplished without implementing surveying at the same time. Otherwise, the number of newly added tax amounts will be very small.

2. If reporting and surveying are carried out at the same time, then concealed land can be found out in full, and the newly added tax amount must be large. However, the use of the new tax must also be separately stipulated according to the conditions of each province, and cannot be generalized.

3. Judging from the current situation in various provinces, there are four uses for the new tax amount in the provinces: one is to reduce the compensation for agricultural surcharges, two is to subsidize county local business expenses, three is to repay outstanding provincial debts, and four is to reserve it for important construction projects throughout the province. All of these must be considered and allocated by the provinces.

4. This item should be revised as follows:

"The central government should clearly stipulate that 40% of the newly added tax amount from this investigation and reporting will be used for important construction projects in the provinces, and 60% will be retained for local business expenses and used to offset surcharges as an incentive."

(3) For Part D, please consider the following points:

1. The item of allowing to reduce or increase tax amounts appropriately for those who report on time or delay their reporting is intended to provide material incentives and punishments for reporters. However, increasing or decreasing tax amounts means increasing or decreasing the burden on the people, which is of utmost importance and should be carefully considered. There are many other methods of rewards and punishments, and there is no need to change the tax amount to avoid generating malpractices.

2. This item should be revised as follows:

"Those who report within the prescribed time limit will not be charged any fees. Those who delay their reporting will be fined 50 cents per acre for handling fees (the penalty for increasing rewards and punishments is clear. It seems to be better to stipulate this than to change the tax amount). Land that is not reported will be deemed to have lost its property rights. All transfers, mortgages, and inheritance will be valid only with the land investigation and reporting certificate."

(4) For Part E, please consider the following points:

1. The conditions for submitting registers are different in each county. Some can be submitted, some cannot be submitted, and some have maps and registers mixed up and indistinguishable, the registers are scattered, and the secret copies of the registers are also unclear. It is difficult to completely submit these old registers; even if they are all submitted, they are useless. The reporting register is fundamentally different from the old tax register, and there is no way to verify them. If you want to force a verification, it will inevitably take many personnel and many days, and the verification result will mostly be inconsistent. Then what to go to and what to save, and what register to use as a basis? It is useless to create disturbances.

2. This item should originally be cancelled; however, in order to passively eliminate obstacles to reporting, it is still necessary to keep it.

(B) Regarding the Proposal to Reduce Land Tax Surcharges:

The various articles in the general outline of measures proposed in this proposal are generally appropriate; however, there is still something to consider, which is the standard for reducing land tax. According to item B in the proposal, there are words such as "the total amount of land tax surcharge shall not exceed the original tax", that is, the verification and reduction of the surcharge is based on the original tax as the standard. However, the level of the original tax varies from province to province, and even within a province, the counties are different from each other. Taking Jiangsu Province as an example, the original silver and rice taxes are different. Generally speaking, the average tax in the counties under the jurisdiction of Suzhou is 9.1 liters per mu; 8 liters per mu in Songjiang; 6 liters per mu in Changzhou; and Jingjiang is the lightest, with only a little over 2 liters per mu; 3.5 liters per mu in Zhenjiang; 2.6 liters per mu in Jiading and Baoshan in Taicang; Chongming has no tax, and Taicang is the only one that moves, which is the same as Suzhou. However, the reduction is even greater in various counties in Jiangbei. Combining the silver tax, the Suzhou, Songjiang, Changzhou, Zhenjiang, and Taicang counties are different, and the counties among them are also different from each other. The disparity in grain tax and the complexity of the tax laws are almost impossible to investigate. The disparity in the land tax laws in various counties in Jiangsu Province, the heavy and light burdens, and the reduction of tax trends in the former Qing Dynasty, originated from this. According to the original silver and rice tax, the county's heavy and light tax amounts are different: for example, Nantong has an original tax as high as one yuan per mu; others such as Shanghai 82 cents, Qingpu Songjiang 76 cents, Wu County 75 cents, Jinshan 74 cents, Fengxian Chuansha Changshu, are all as high as 71 cents or more; and Zhenjiang is as high as 62 cents per mu, Jurong is only 30 cents, Jiangning is only 26 cents; also, in counties such as Chongming Qidong Gaoyou Lianshui, the highest tax rate of the original tax per mu is less than 10 cents. And in Gaoyou County, the highest tax rate of the original tax per mu is only 16 cents, and the total original tax of the county is 70,000 yuan, and the surtax is as high as 1.37 million yuan, exceeding the tax by more than 16 times; and according to the 1% standard, the total amount of original tax and surtax has not exceeded the limit. It can be seen that the level of the original tax in each county and the disparity in the proportion of its surtax, its limits and standards, are difficult to stipulate. This is the result of observing one province.

Now, looking at the whole country again, the original land tax in various provinces is very different. Generally speaking, the provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang are the highest, Sichuan's advance levy is the largest, Hebei's taxes are very light, Hunan and Hubei's original tax is light and the surcharges are heavy, Shandong's levy is 4 yuan per tael of silver, and Hebei's levy is only a little over 2 yuan per tael; although Jiangsu's levy is only 2 yuan and 5 cents per tael, the levy on rice is as high as 5 yuan per shih, which is a phenomenon that is absent in various provinces in North China. Therefore, the total amount of busy transport and original tax is still heavier than in other provinces. Unfortunately, there are not many reference materials in the market, and it is impossible to list all the examples of the disparity in the heavy and light taxes in various provinces across the country. As mentioned above, it is enough to see that the conditions in various provinces cannot be forced to be the same.

Under the actual conditions of the different provinces and counties, the method of verifying and reducing land tax surcharges, in addition to separately determining them according to the economic and social realities of the rural areas of each province, the most important standard for reducing taxes, in my humble opinion, should not be uniformly based on "the surtax shall not exceed the original tax", but should be carefully verified according to the people's burden in each province. The areas where the original tax on silver and rice is too heavy, the surtax should be strictly limited to below the original tax, or at most can only be equal to the original tax; the counties where the original tax on silver and rice is too light may be appropriately increased compared to the original tax, in order to correct the past disparity in the original silver and rice tax and to achieve fairness in the burden.

The above-mentioned are only the proposals themselves that the Ministry of Finance has sought opinions from various provinces and cities, and it is only intended to express

my personal ideals for reorganizing land tax in one in ten thousand. However, the national land tax reorganization problem is extremely complex, and to make a detailed judgment is probably not within the scope of this topic. I will wait for another day to write a detailed discussion on it. I hope that those with lofty ideals who are determined to reform land tax will immediately study this proposal of the Ministry of Finance in detail and make detailed distinctions, so that the most urgent and deeply rooted land tax problem in the country can be obtained with the most complete reorganization method for the decision of the financial conference, and it can be implemented uniformly throughout the country.

Drafted on May 1, 23rd year, at the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance

On Banks Operating Real Estate 292

— Junsi

In the past year, the flourishing of banking businesses reached its peak. Looking at the year as a whole, the establishment of new banks and branches numbered no less than dozens, and each of these dozens of banks profited greatly, with surpluses ranging from tens of thousands to hundreds of thousands. On the surface, this phenomenon is certainly a celebratory event. However, if we examine it carefully, it is not difficult to realize that this phenomenon is actually an abnormal development of banks and a reflection of an unsound economic and social organization. This is because the banking industry absolutely cannot thrive independently, divorced from the closely related and interdependent industrial and commercial sectors. Therefore, its impact not only provides no benefit to the struggling people but also poses a significant harm to the entire society. Upon investigation, the reason for this is that since the global economic depression, industry and commerce have been sluggish, and all sectors have declined. Banks have felt a lack of outlets for investment, facing difficulties everywhere. The accelerated bankruptcy of rural areas and the unrest in the interior have further concentrated funds in cities, flowing into banks. Bankers, feeling the difficulty of investing funds and witnessing the influx of idle capital from various places, have had no choice but to flock to government bonds and real estate. In this situation, investing in government bonds and buying and selling real estate have become the main businesses of various banks during this abnormal development. This is because everyone knows that investing in government bonds is more secure than investing in any other enterprise, and buying and selling real estate is easier to profit from than any other enterprise. However, investing in government bonds directly takes from the country and indirectly takes from the people, and its harmful impact on the development of the national economy is self-evident. The same is true for real estate. On the surface, it stimulates the market and promotes urban prosperity, but in reality, it causes real estate prices to skyrocket, making life increasingly difficult for the general public and plunging the economic and social order into extreme instability and unease.

In addition to their inherent banking operations, banks engaging in the real estate business is a recent phenomenon. Nowadays, most banks in Shanghai have established real estate departments, staffed by experienced personnel who specialize in this area. Their business operations are roughly similar to those of ordinary real estate companies, and can be roughly divided into three points: (1) Real estate sales and purchases; (2) Handling mortgages; (3) Property leasing. Real estate sales and purchases can be further divided into two categories: (A) When a bank is entrusted by a shareholder to find a piece of land that meets certain conditions, the bank pays attention, carefully looking for suitable locations. If a certain plot of land is suitable and the price is low, the bank can earn a large commission upon completion of the transaction as compensation. Conversely, if a property owner has land for sale, they can also entrust the bank's real estate department to handle it. If it can be sold, the bank can collect a commission as usual. (B) Banks often observe that the market in a certain area will become increasingly prosperous, and land prices will become increasingly expensive. Therefore, banks take the opportunity to buy in at low prices and then wait for the right opportunity to sell at a good price. The amount of profit earned in a short period is far beyond what other enterprises can hope to achieve. (2) Handling mortgages - When owners of real estate encounter important matters and urgently need cash for turnover, they often mortgage their properties to others. The proceeds from the mortgage are used to solve their immediate needs. In this regard, banks use their surplus funds to engage in large-scale mortgage business, either guaranteeing interest and redemption, or allocating rent for interest, and the high interest rates often reach 8% or 9% per month. (3) Property leasing - Banks manage the collection and settlement of rent for property owners and charge a handling fee accordingly. In addition, we can observe a common trend in the banking sector in recent years, namely, banks owning their own real estate. Looking at the bustling urban areas of Shanghai, the magnificent high-rise buildings that reach into the clouds are all owned by various banks (although the land on which some bank buildings stand may not be owned by the bank but leased, they are still self-built). The banks themselves certainly have limited needs and do not need a large number of offices. Therefore, in each bank building, except for the three floors used by the bank itself, the floors above the first and second floors are all used as offices for rent. In this situation, it is inevitable that they can collect considerable rent every month, and the success of their budget is an undeniable fact. However, we have observed that this trend in the banking sector is gradually showing signs of decline.

Undoubtedly, in addition to convenient transportation and excellent location, many bank offices are empty and unattended. This phenomenon proves that there is an oversupply of offices, which are entering a state of failure. At the same time, we also know that the sluggishness of industry and commerce has made most people reluctant to engage in business, and they are hesitant to move forward. The bankers are only concerned about their own interests and arbitrarily raise rents, causing

tenants to bear a heavy burden. Therefore, we dare to say that banks may still be able to maintain a considerable degree of success in building their own buildings and renting out offices at present. However, if this trend continues and banks do not seek to develop their business in other ways, the future danger will be unavoidable.

We have seen that in the socio-economic structure, nothing is more closely related to the people than the huge expense of rent in their expenditures. The high cost of rent poses a great threat to the general public. For businesses, the high rent makes it difficult to operate, and as a result, a large number of businesses feel unable to sustain themselves and are in a precarious state. This phenomenon was most evident at the end of last year. Although, generally speaking, the origin of this phenomenon is influenced by the global economic depression, the high rent, which small people cannot afford, is also a major reason. As for private homes, on the one hand, it is due to the soaring land prices, and on the other hand, it is due to rural bankruptcy. The rural population is gradually leaving the countryside and seeking a livelihood in the cities, so the rents have also increased to the extreme. In this situation, special terms such as "second landlords" and "third landlords" have emerged. Often, seven or eight families live in one house, with a large population, neglecting sanitation, and the problem of housing cannot be solved to the extreme. Therefore, some people feel their own pain and stand up to cry out loudly, demanding to get rid of it. Therefore, the enthusiastic promotion of rent reduction movements and the resulting response are not accidental but inevitable facts.

At the same time, we also see that real estate is not a legitimate business for banks. Here, we should ask a question: Is it because of the lack of outlets for funds that banks should not think about breaking the deadlock and specialize in some illegitimate government bonds and real estate? Although banks' buying and selling of real estate on behalf of customers is a service to society, it should be noted that the people being served are only a small number of wealthy people in society. From another perspective, banks are public service institutions and should not ignore the welfare of the masses in order to gain a little current benefit. As for the buying and selling of real estate, it all depends on

speculation and trickery, which is not a business policy that bankers should adopt. Secondly, as for mortgages, everyone knows that real estate is immovable property. The degree of danger for banks to accept immovable property as collateral for loans is extremely deep. Again, as for property leasing, we don't want to say anything, but we have seen banks going down a path that banks should not be going down. We feel that banks should change their policies in the future and shift the power of the real estate department to seek the welfare of the general public in order to solve the housing problems of the people in society.

Whether in theory or in practice, this is not an impossible thing. Banks use surplus funds to consider the situation in commercial urban areas, buy or lease suitable land, and build a large number of urban houses for rent. The construction of these urban houses does not require magnificence, but only practicality, and the most important thing is that banks should reduce their rents to the lowest possible level within the scope of possibility to reduce the burden of merchants in these exorbitant taxes. This move directly opens up a path for merchants and indirectly promotes commercial prosperity and market revitalization. Even for

the banks themselves, it can make their position more solid and their reputation even more outstanding. Secondly, they should build new village-style residences in the suburbs that are slightly away from the city but have convenient transportation. These residences are either suitable for middle-class families or for lower-class people to live in, in order to solve the housing problems of the general public. Investigating this action, it is certainly a great contribution to society, and for the banks themselves, it is not unprofitable to collect considerable rent every month. However, it is undeniable that the profits obtained are not as abundant as buying and selling real estate, but we know that a bank has a considerable responsibility to society and cannot ignore its more important and great mission for the sake of greed for current small profits. Therefore, I think banks should show us some achievements in serving society, reducing the burden on the people, and solving the housing problems of the people. This is a very important task, and I hope that the banking community will not neglect it!

Silk and Tea: Spring Silkworms Startled by Thunderstorms 298

Short and temporary, with no major adverse effects

(Liangzhu) The Liangzhu area of Hangzhou is also an improved sericulture area. This year, many farmers hatch improved breeds, while silkworm farmers in places such as Liuxia also raise native breeds due to economic reasons. However, due to the bad weather, the seeds of native breeds are unsound and have weak resistance, resulting in a loss of 60-70%. The silkworm ants in the improved areas have undergone scientific new methods of full relief by instructors, and there have been no major changes in the silkworm ants. When the weather turned sunny and warm during the first dormancy, the temperature was suitable, and the silkworm ants developed smoothly. The early batch of silkworms has been on the cocooning frames for four or five days, and in another two hundred days, they can be taken off the frames. However, the heavy thunderstorm last night for half an hour caused the silkworms on the cocooning frames to stop spinning silk. Fortunately, the thunder was not loud, and they resumed cocooning as usual after a while.

(Yuanhua) The improved breeds hatched by farmers in Jinshidun and other places hatched later due to the cold weather. During the second and third dormancy, the temperature was insufficient, and the continuous rain for ten days caused the humidity to be too high, and the silkworms changed. The instructors worked hard to coordinate and provide universal assistance, and finally used human power to control the bad weather. When the third dormancy was sufficient, the weather turned sunny and warm. During the first dormancy, the silkworm ants developed healthily. The early silkworms have all gone up the mountain to cocoon, and in three or four days, they can be taken off the frames. Last night, there was heavy rain, coupled with huge thunder. The silkworms on the cocooning frames must not hear thunder. Fortunately, it was very temporary and the thunder was still small, but the spinning of silk stopped and soon returned to normal.

(Shuanglin) This year is also an improved sericulture area, and farmers are raising improved breeds. However, due to the bad weather, hatching was late. During the first two dormancies, the instructors ran around to rescue them, working extremely hard. When entering the third dormancy, the weather was clear and sunny, and the silkworm ants developed smoothly. The early batch has been in the third dormancy and has sufficient mulberry leaves, and some have started to wake up from the first dormancy. The late batch has also been in the third dormancy and has been feeding on mulberry leaves for many days. Last night, there was a heavy thunderstorm, but the fresh mulberry leaves stored in advance by the instructors were enough for one day and night of feed, and there was no impact. However, the early batch of native silkworms raised by farmers suffered heavy damage during the second dormancy, and there were few remaining silkworms.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talking

Going to the Northwest 301

— Ya Fei

Because of the bankruptcy of rural areas in all provinces of China, and frequent foreign invasions requiring urgent self-salvation, the authorities have turned their attention to the Northwest. Consequently, people from both official and public circles are unanimously and enthusiastically clamoring to go to the Northwest, to go to the Northwest. However, simply shouting to go to the Northwest will not make it happen; developing the Northwest requires grand plans and massive funding. It also requires the determination and hard work of many people, starting with the rural areas and implementing measures based on the situation. Otherwise, the result will still be more people shouting than going, and even less actually doing anything, which of course will be nonexistent. The Northwest is located on the border, with a vast area and sparse population. However, due to its fertile soil, agricultural production is extremely rich. Unfortunately, years of natural disasters have turned the Northwest farmers into a group of lamenting victims! Furthermore, in recent years, frequent internal turmoil and foreign invasions, coupled with the authorities being unable to effectively manage or adequately care for the region, have indeed been major contributing factors. Not long ago, key figures of the National Government, such as Shao Lizi, Song Ziwen, and Dai Chuanxian, personally went to the Northwest to conduct thorough inspections. Several concrete measures have now been proposed for the construction of the Northwest: (1) Irrigation, as the Northwest has suffered from drought for a long time, irrigation is the most urgent task for developing the Northwest. (2) Animal husbandry is a supplementary industry to agriculture and forestry, and is beneficial to agriculture; therefore, it cannot be neglected. (3) Prevention and control of animal diseases; with animal husbandry, the prevention and control of animal diseases is extremely important. (4) Rural cooperation, improving methods, strengthening forces, to enhance the foundation of agriculture.

We have no doubts about the above measures for developing the Northwest; however, the points I want to make now are not such simple matters; rather, they are some opinions that I wish to respectfully offer to the authorities developing the Northwest. Undoubtedly, these are tasks we should do before going to the Northwest, preparations we should make before discussing the construction of the Northwest.

How can we develop the Northwest? This is a huge question; however, the question itself is always worth studying. According to my suggestion, to develop the Northwest, we only need to utilize prisoners and the poor, sending them to the Northwest to engage in the hard labor of reclaiming wasteland; on one hand, the government should allocate huge funds to undertake various construction projects, and at the same time, it is hoped that the financial community and capitalists will invest as much as possible in agricultural and forestry industries or construction projects, so as to promote their development and prosperity. As for commerce, education, sanitation, public security, transportation, water conservancy, agricultural reclamation, and other construction projects, they should all be established and promoted separately. All prisoners selected to go to the Northwest should have their sentences appropriately reduced by a certain percentage, and after their sentences are completed, they should be given appropriate jobs separately. Each poor person should be given a few acres of mountain land and a few acres of farmland; during the construction period, they can freely cultivate the land, without paying land rent or land prices, and without being subject to any taxes. It is also advisable to consider the situation and establish industrial factories, recruiting unemployed workers to go there to work: in order to advance both relief and construction.

When it comes to developing the Northwest, it should be divided into several steps, decided upon, and then carried out step by step; the first step is preparation, the second step is trial implementation, and the third step is implementation. After these three steps are completed, we can take a further step in construction and improvement. I think that with this method, although I dare not say that it will achieve twice the result with half the effort, at least it will have considerable success.

Lost Check 302

— Yi Peng

Since the New Life Movement was launched, whether it's carrying lanterns or attending meetings, if you have this "hard expansion" badge, you can pass without hindrance. I heard that although grass skirt striptease was banned, those swaggering Russian women are still performing on stage, with advertisers cleverly calling it fitness, which is naturally also part of the New Life Movement.

Now that "Peach Blossom River" and "Dance Partner's Song" are banned, why not say that this is the New Life Movement, promoting healthy and beautiful voices, so that these charming and delicate famous songs can be heard in the world a few more times!

The so-called tricks are known to everyone, but each has its own skill. In the past, when the Northern Expedition was completed, opening your eyes revealed a "Sun Yat-sen World." Barber shops were called "Sun Yat-sen," Western restaurants were also "Sun Yat-sen," "Sun Yat-sen" rubber shoes, and "Sun Yat-sen" Hong Kong beef. Compared with today's New Life Movement, it can be seen that mankind has exhausted its intelligence.

Last year there was a time called the "Prize-Winning Cigarette" era, where ten empty packs could be exchanged for a prize coupon, with top prizes of several thousand or ten thousand yuan, etc. Later, the government, fearing that it would steal the business of aviation lottery tickets, ordered a ban. But this kind of good business has to find a way to continue; so now someone has invented the "lost check," and there's no way to stop it. In a few days, the cigarettes handed over from others all had that bird-like, non-bird-like trademark. After all, everyone loves money, a huge sum of a thousand yuan. Since you're smoking anyway, why not smoke XX brand! And the Tax Department of the Ministry of Finance only issued an order saying that this move might cause other cigarette factories to follow suit and hold cash prize giveaways, which would violate the department's regulations, so they would no longer be allowed to publish the winners' names in the newspapers, etc. However, the company claims that these "lost checks" are invented for the sake of the company's reputation and will be redeemed with half the amount in cash, so they will definitely continue to do so. Looking at it this way, that bird-like, non-bird-like trademark will definitely spread like wildfire! Although the New Life Movement prohibits smoking, the cigarette company has a new invention that is unprecedented and unparalleled, which is also the newest life in the sound of the New Life Movement. The old cigarette companies that used to appeal with prize coupons, hurry up and move forward! As long as you're not stupid, you're bound to have a more wonderful trick than the "lost check" to promote your goods. I'm paying attention to this big advertisement every day!

Thoughts on the Far Eastern Games 303

— Bai Rong

Since the opening of the Far Eastern Games, our country has had little hope in anything other than soccer, especially in track and field, which has been almost completely wiped out. It's truly regrettable. However, news came that our country's women's swimming, through the efforts of Yang Xiuqiong and others, had won several championships in a row. Not only were those who care about sports excited to hear this, but every one of us Chinese people had to jump for joy three hundred times. Newspapers also said: Filipinos criticized our country's female athletes for coming not to compete in sports, but to compete in beauty. This completely overturned these ridiculous criticisms. This aroused some small thoughts in me: The purpose of sports is to cultivate a strong physique. In addition to this, it can also cultivate morality, train intelligence, and create a healthy and beautiful physique. This is a well-known fact. In the new era of the twentieth century, the old standards for measuring beauty and ugliness are no longer applicable. The frail physique of the oriental type like Lin Daiyu has become something that has been eliminated and discarded. In this era, what is held up as our standard of beauty is a healthy, strong, and active spirit. But this can only be obtained through diligent exercise and attention to health, and it can never be achieved through artificial affectation. Applying Parisian perfume, applying scarlet nail polish, adding beauty marks, and perming hair are just taking the decorative techniques of the feudal era and re-enacting them in a new way. Although people are wearing the clothes of "modernity," their bones are no different from those of women of the Lin Daiyu type. Extravagance, weakness, and frivolity are everywhere, driving backward and doing "corrupting" work everywhere. This phenomenon is already a common sight in cities.

Therefore, we hope that the education authorities can, on the one hand, curb the extravagant and frivolous academic atmosphere, and on the other hand, promote healthy and beautiful sports. In the sports field, we should pay special attention to the cultivation of true strong physiques and the formation of true competitive spirit, and spread the true meaning of sports to the minds of students. As for the athletes who represent the entire nation in international sports games, they should be especially cautious, because their every move is related to the reputation of the entire country. Not to mention the past, even in this Far Eastern Games, the Filipinos' slander of our female athletes is of course too arrogant, but we should ask ourselves, do our country's "female athletes" really have places that cause misunderstandings? Why do they mock us alone and not the female athletes of other countries? Because of this, I remembered the story of a female ball team member who was ridiculed by foreigners for applying powder on her legs when playing ball, and I felt even more that people in society should loudly call for curbing this bad trend. The extravagance and frivolity of one team member will affect all the athletes, and behind all the athletes stands the entire nation. Athletes representing China should not only sew the national flag on their clothes, but also sew it on their entire hearts. Only in this way will they be serious and not think that this is a trip abroad to show off and compete in beauty, and as a result only bring back ridicule and no trophies!

This time, Yang Xiuqiong and others were able to compete with strength and bring glory to the country, which is worthy of admiration, but I did not erase the other female athletes with success or failure. Taking volleyball as an example, the female athletes' crying after the defeat, although their competitive spirit was thwarted, can also be seen in their patriotic enthusiasm. I hope that after the athletes return to China, they can encourage each other, avoid the temptation of vanity, and painstakingly forge a stronger physique. Healthy beauty is genuine beauty without discount, and the glory of sufficient physical strength is genuine glory. If you truly understand this, then scarlet rouge, perfume, and lipstick will all become meaningless.

On Nurseries and Public Childcare 304

— Shi Shi

Recently, the authorities in this city established a relatively large-scale nursery. This, in terms of "social construction," is undoubtedly very valuable. In the past, similar places in our country, such as the inherent infant homes, baby protection centers, and universal nurseries, were mostly set up to accommodate abandoned, ownerless infants and children. They were merely charitable undertakings operated under a narrow sense of humanitarianism. Pure childcare institutions with socio-educational ideals like this seem to be groundbreaking in our country. The theoretical basis for setting up nurseries is generally based on the European and American theory of "public childcare." This has close relationships with issues such as social evolution, women's economy, and infant education and upbringing. Therefore, if the establishment of nurseries in this city this time is not merely a formalistic, superficial decoration, we may as well assume that it is the first step in the widespread implementation of public childcare. In that case, this issue seems to be worthy of attention.

Public childcare is quite active in Europe and America, and can be effectively implemented in Soviet Russia, achieving effective results. Their facilities for public childcare are particularly meticulous, stipulating that a public childcare area must be specially set up for every certain number of people, including enrollment offices, fetal centers, lactation centers, infant hospitals, infant playgrounds, kindergartens, children's sports fields, children's health rooms, children's small craft workshops, children's libraries, children's reformatories, etc. Experts are also selected and hired to organize children's research institutes, studying children's physiology, children's psychology, children's education, and children's training at any time, implementing them in practice, in order to achieve the most perfect and beautiful state. Such large-scale public childcare institutions will directly give us great yearning. Regarding the theoretical system advocating public childcare, in Europe and America, it can be roughly divided into two schools: one is the socialist school, represented by people such as George Bernard Shaw. They particularly focus on the efficiency of social evolution, believing that women are "social beings" and not members attached to the family. Therefore, they advocate reforming the family system, liberating women's status, in order to provide for social tasks, and the responsibility of raising children should naturally be borne by society. The second is the feminist school, represented by people such as Charlotte Perkins Gilman. They focus on women's own rights and interests, advocating women's economic independence and occupational liberation, using public childcare to regulate their family burdens. The arguments of these two schools each have a theoretical basis, and although their positions are different, their conclusions on the implementation of public childcare are similar.

The position of this city's nursery establishment this time is probably no exception to the above two schools. As a superficial and inexperienced person, the author certainly cannot make any criticisms in terms of theory. However, based on our observation of the current social situation in our country, national economy, cultural level, and various aspects of family concepts, whether it is urgent to promote public childcare, I feel that there are still points of doubt that are worth discussing in detail.

Due to the economic collapse and the low cultural level, the social structure of modern China fully shows its deformed morbid state. Women are engaged in occupations, but in reality, it is only a short-term youth. The so-called task of following society is only a dream of a clear autumn. Some people say that marriage is the only profession for women, although it is a joke, it is actually the truth. Then, since the current society cannot retain considerable positions for mothers who have children, this kind of nursery dedicated to childcare has already lost its necessity of existence. Moreover, women have a natural "maternal duty" towards their children. This maternal duty is an absolute obligation in ethics, a relative obligation to society, and children are the mainstay of the future society. Women raising children to be physically and mentally healthy are also serving society. The true value of this task, compared with the profession of being a vase in an institution or a living advertisement in a mall, is like the difference between heaven and earth. Then the existence of nurseries has obviously lost its theoretical basis.

Furthermore, children and families have an inseparable relationship. Children are the happy center of the family. Couples often use children as a tool to maintain emotions, and having children and grandchildren around the knees can create family happiness. John Dewey said, "Without children, the house becomes just a building." Therefore, promoting public childcare will inevitably destroy the integrity of the family. Only a few adults are left in the family, which becomes a cold world, and what is the fun of life? And the family is the paradise of children's lives. Parental love is the only food in children's lives, otherwise, it is difficult to survive. Now, wanting to entrust weak infants to unrelated third parties is truly a great cruel act. According to statistics from the city of Paris, France, the mortality rate of public childcare children is more than three times higher than that of ordinary children. Then, doesn't the nursery become a great crisis? Moreover, in the current state of economic turmoil and poverty in China, families below the middle class will definitely have no extra money to pay a childcare fee to the nursery every month. If there are more than two children, it is far less economical than breastfeeding on their own. Therefore, the establishment of nurseries, in fact, only opens the door wide for those frivolous playboys, and the result may become the tail of illegitimate children and adulterous children; this is too far from the original intention of running nurseries.

The above is the author's personal subjective view, and perhaps some people will ridicule it as being outdated. But I believe my attitude is very sincere.

— Forget Myself

Nature lends me her pen 本埠三馬大塊頭丑史大兴问罪之师
